> <a name="19:78:20">78:20</a> Yes, he struck a rock and water flowed out,
> streams gushed forth.
> But can he also give us food?
> Will he provide meat for his people?”
> <a name="19:78:21">78:21</a> When the Lord heard this, he was furious.
> A fire broke out against Jacob,
> and his anger flared up against Israel,
> <a name="19:78:22">78:22</a> because they did not have faith in God,
> and did not trust his ability to deliver them.
> <a name="19:78:23">78:23</a> He gave a command to the clouds above,
> and opened the doors in the sky.
> <a name="19:78:24">78:24</a> He rained down manna for them to eat;
> he gave them the grain of heaven.
> <a name="19:78:25">78:25</a> Man ate the food of the mighty ones.
> He sent them more than enough to eat.
> <a name="19:78:26">78:26</a> He brought the east wind through the sky,
> and by his strength led forth the south wind.
> <a name="19:78:27">78:27</a> He rained down meat on them like dust,
> birds as numerous as the sand on the seashores.
> <a name="19:78:28">78:28</a> He caused them to fall right in the middle of their camp,
> all around their homes.
> <a name="19:78:29">78:29</a> They ate until they were stuffed;
> he gave them what they desired.
> <a name="19:78:30">78:30</a> They were not yet filled up,
> their food was still in their mouths,
> <a name="19:78:31">78:31</a> when the anger of God flared up against them.
> He killed some of the strongest of them;
> he brought the young men of Israel to their knees.
> <a name="19:78:32">78:32</a> Despite all this, they continued to sin,
> and did not trust him to do amazing things.
> <a name="19:78:33">78:33</a> So he caused them to die unsatisfied
> and filled with terror.
> <a name="19:78:34">78:34</a> When he struck them down, they sought his favor;
> they turned back and longed for God.
> <a name="19:78:35">78:35</a> They remembered that God was their protector,
> and that the sovereign God was their deliverer.
> <a name="19:78:36">78:36</a> But they deceived him with their words,
> and lied to him.
> <a name="19:78:37">78:37</a> They were not really committed to him,
> and they were unfaithful to his covenant.
> <a name="19:78:38">78:38</a> Yet he is compassionate.
> He forgives sin and does not destroy.
> He often holds back his anger,
> and does not stir up his fury.
> <a name="19:78:39">78:39</a> He remembered that they were made of flesh,
> and were like a wind that blows past and does not return.
> <a name="19:78:40">78:40</a> How often they rebelled against him in the wilderness,
> and insulted him in the desert!
> <a name="19:78:41">78:41</a> They again challenged God,
> and offended the sovereign king of Israel.
> <a name="19:78:42">78:42</a> They did not remember what he had done,
> how he delivered them from the enemy,
> <a name="19:78:43">78:43</a> when he performed his awesome deeds in Egypt,
> and his acts of judgment in the region of Zoan.
> <a name="19:78:44">78:44</a> He turned their rivers into blood,
> and they could not drink from their streams.
> <a name="19:78:45">78:45</a> He sent swarms of biting insects against them,
> as well as frogs that overran their land.
> <a name="19:78:46">78:46</a> He gave their crops to the grasshopper,
> the fruit of their labor to the locust.
> <a name="19:78:47">78:47</a> He destroyed their vines with hail,
> and their sycamore-fig trees with driving rain.
> <a name="19:78:48">78:48</a> He rained hail down on their cattle,
> and hurled lightning bolts down on their livestock.
> <a name="19:78:49">78:49</a> His raging anger lashed out against them,
> He sent fury, rage, and trouble
> as messengers who bring disaster.
> <a name="19:78:50">78:50</a> He sent his anger in full force;
> he did not spare them from death;
> he handed their lives over to destruction.
> <a name="19:78:51">78:51</a> He struck down all the firstborn in Egypt,
> the firstfruits of their reproductive power in the tents of Ham.
> <a name="19:78:52">78:52</a> Yet he brought out his people like sheep;
> he led them through the wilderness like a flock.
> <a name="19:78:53">78:53</a> He guided them safely along,
> while the sea covered their enemies.
> <a name="19:78:54">78:54</a> He brought them to the border of his holy land,
> to this mountainous land which his right hand acquired.
> <a name="19:78:55">78:55</a> He drove the nations out from before them;
> he assigned them their tribal allotments
> and allowed the tribes of Israel to settle down.
> <a name="19:78:56">78:56</a> Yet they challenged and defied the Sovereign God,
> and did not obey his commands.
> <a name="19:78:57">78:57</a> They were unfaithful and acted as treacherously as their ancestors;
> they were as unreliable as a malfunctioning bow.
> <a name="19:78:58">78:58</a> They made him angry with their pagan shrines,
> and made him jealous with their idols.
> <a name="19:78:59">78:59</a> God heard and was angry;
> he completely rejected Israel.
> <a name="19:78:60">78:60</a> He abandoned the sanctuary at Shiloh,
> the tent where he lived among men.
> <a name="19:78:61">78:61</a> He allowed the symbol of his strong presence to be captured;
> he gave the symbol of his splendor into the hand of the enemy.
> <a name="19:78:62">78:62</a> He delivered his people over to the sword,
> and was angry with his chosen nation.
> <a name="19:78:63">78:63</a> Fire consumed their young men,
> and their virgins remained unmarried.
> <a name="19:78:64">78:64</a> Their priests fell by the sword,
> but their widows did not weep.
> <a name="19:78:65">78:65</a> But then the sovereign Master awoke from his sleep;
> he was like a warrior in a drunken rage.
> <a name="19:78:66">78:66</a> He drove his enemies back;
> he made them a permanent target for insults.
> <a name="19:78:67">78:67</a> He rejected the tent of Joseph;
> he did not choose the tribe of Ephraim.
> <a name="19:78:68">78:68</a> He chose the tribe of Judah,
> and Mount Zion, which he loves.
> <a name="19:78:69">78:69</a> He made his sanctuary as enduring as the heavens above;
> as secure as the earth, which he established permanently.
> <a name="19:78:70">78:70</a> He chose David, his servant,
> and took him from the sheepfolds.
> <a name="19:78:71">78:71</a> He took him away from following the mother sheep,
> and made him the shepherd of Jacob, his people,
> and of Israel, his chosen nation.
> <a name="19:78:72">78:72</a> David cared for them with pure motives;
> he led them with skill.

### Psalm 79

A psalm of Asaph.

> <a name="19:79:1">79:1</a> O God, foreigners have invaded your chosen land;
> they have polluted your holy temple
> and turned Jerusalem into a heap of ruins.
> <a name="19:79:2">79:2</a> They have given the corpses of your servants
> to the birds of the sky;
> the flesh of your loyal followers
> to the beasts of the earth.
> <a name="19:79:3">79:3</a> They have made their blood flow like water
> all around Jerusalem, and there is no one to bury them.
> <a name="19:79:4">79:4</a> We have become an object of disdain to our neighbors;
> those who live on our borders taunt and insult us.
> <a name="19:79:5">79:5</a> How long will this go on, O Lord?
> Will you stay angry forever?
> How long will your rage burn like fire?
> <a name="19:79:6">79:6</a> Pour out your anger on the nations that do not acknowledge you,
> on the kingdoms that do not pray to you!
> <a name="19:79:7">79:7</a> For they have devoured Jacob
> and destroyed his home.
> <a name="19:79:8">79:8</a> Do not hold us accountable for the sins of earlier generations!
> Quickly send your compassion our way,
> for we are in serious trouble!
> <a name="19:79:9">79:9</a> Help us, O God, our deliverer!
> For the sake of your glorious reputation, rescue us!
> Forgive our sins for the sake of your reputation!
> <a name="19:79:10">79:10</a> Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?”
> Before our very eyes may the shed blood of your servants
> be avenged among the nations!
> <a name="19:79:11">79:11</a> Listen to the painful cries of the prisoners!
> Use your great strength to set free those condemned to die!
> <a name="19:79:12">79:12</a> Pay back our neighbors in full!
> May they be insulted the same way they insulted you, O sovereign Master!
> <a name="19:79:13">79:13</a> Then we, your people, the sheep of your pasture,
> will continually thank you.
> We will tell coming generations of your praiseworthy acts.

### Psalm 80

For the music director; according to the shushan-eduth style; a psalm of Asaph.

> <a name="19:80:1">80:1</a> O shepherd of Israel, pay attention,
> you who lead Joseph like a flock of sheep!
> You who sit enthroned above the winged angels, reveal your splendor!
> <a name="19:80:2">80:2</a> In the sight of Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasseh reveal your power!
> Come and deliver us!
> <a name="19:80:3">80:3</a> O God, restore us!
> Smile on us! Then we will be delivered!
> <a name="19:80:4">80:4</a> O Lord God, invincible warrior!
> How long will you remain angry at your people while they pray to you?
> <a name="19:80:5">80:5</a> You have given them tears as food;
> you have made them drink tears by the measure.
> <a name="19:80:6">80:6</a> You have made our neighbors dislike us,
> and our enemies insult us.
> <a name="19:80:7">80:7</a> O God, invincible warrior, restore us!
> Smile on us! Then we will be delivered!
> <a name="19:80:8">80:8</a> You uprooted a vine from Egypt;
> you drove out nations and transplanted it.
> <a name="19:80:9">80:9</a> You cleared the ground for it;
> it took root,
> and filled the land.
> <a name="19:80:10">80:10</a> The mountains were covered by its shadow,
> the highest cedars by its branches.
> <a name="19:80:11">80:11</a> Its branches reached the Mediterranean Sea,
> and its shoots the Euphrates River.
> <a name="19:80:12">80:12</a> Why did you break down its walls,
> so that all who pass by pluck its fruit?
> <a name="19:80:13">80:13</a> The wild boars of the forest ruin it;
> the insects of the field feed on it.
> <a name="19:80:14">80:14</a> O God, invincible warrior, come back!
> Look down from heaven and take notice!
> Take care of this vine,
> <a name="19:80:15">80:15</a> the root your right hand planted,
> the shoot you made to grow!
> <a name="19:80:16">80:16</a> It is burned and cut down.
> They die because you are displeased with them.
> <a name="19:80:17">80:17</a> May you give support to the one you have chosen,
> to the one whom you raised up for yourself!
> <a name="19:80:18">80:18</a> Then we will not turn away from you.
> Revive us and we will pray to you!
> <a name="19:80:19">80:19</a> O Lord God, invincible warrior, restore us!
> Smile on us! Then we will be delivered!

### Psalm 81

For the music director; according to the gittith style; by Asaph.

> <a name="19:81:1">81:1</a> Shout for joy to God, our source of strength!
> Shout out to the God of Jacob!
> <a name="19:81:2">81:2</a> Sing a song and play the tambourine,
> the pleasant sounding harp, and the ten-stringed instrument!
> <a name="19:81:3">81:3</a> Sound the ram’s horn on the day of the new moon,
> and on the day of the full moon when our festival begins.
> <a name="19:81:4">81:4</a> For observing the festival is a requirement for Israel;
> it is an ordinance given by the God of Jacob.
> <a name="19:81:5">81:5</a> He decreed it as a regulation in Joseph,
> when he attacked the land of Egypt.
> I heard a voice I did not recognize.
> <a name="19:81:6">81:6</a> It said: “I removed the burden from his shoulder;
> his hands were released from holding the basket.
> <a name="19:81:7">81:7</a> In your distress you called out and I rescued you.
> I answered you from a dark thundercloud.
> I tested you at the waters of Meribah. (Selah)
> <a name="19:81:8">81:8</a> I said, ‘Listen, my people!
> I will warn you!
> O Israel, if only you would obey me!
> <a name="19:81:9">81:9</a> There must be no other god among you.
> You must not worship a foreign god.
> <a name="19:81:10">81:10</a> I am the Lord, your God,
> the one who brought you out of the land of Egypt.
> Open your mouth wide and I will fill it!’
> <a name="19:81:11">81:11</a> But my people did not obey me;
> Israel did not submit to me.
> <a name="19:81:12">81:12</a> I gave them over to their stubborn desires;
> they did what seemed right to them.
> <a name="19:81:13">81:13</a> If only my people would obey me!
> If only Israel would keep my commands!
> <a name="19:81:14">81:14</a> Then I would quickly subdue their enemies,
> and attack their adversaries.”
> <a name="19:81:15">81:15</a> (May those who hate the Lord cower in fear before him!
> May they be permanently humiliated!)
> <a name="19:81:16">81:16</a> “I would feed Israel the best wheat,
> and would satisfy your appetite with honey from the rocky cliffs.”

### Psalm 82

A psalm of Asaph.

> <a name="19:82:1">82:1</a> God stands in the assembly of El;
> in the midst of the gods he renders judgment.
> <a name="19:82:2">82:2</a> He says, “How long will you make unjust legal decisions
> and show favoritism to the wicked? (Selah)
> <a name="19:82:3">82:3</a> Defend the cause of the poor and the fatherless!
> Vindicate the oppressed and suffering!
> <a name="19:82:4">82:4</a> Rescue the poor and needy!
> Deliver them from the power of the wicked!
> <a name="19:82:5">82:5</a> They neither know nor understand.
> They stumble around in the dark,
> while all the foundations of the earth crumble.
> <a name="19:82:6">82:6</a> I thought, ‘You are gods;
> all of you are sons of the Most High.’
> <a name="19:82:7">82:7</a> Yet you will die like mortals;
> you will fall like all the other rulers.”
> <a name="19:82:8">82:8</a> Rise up, O God, and execute judgment on the earth!
> For you own all the nations.

### Psalm 83

A song, a psalm of Asaph.

> <a name="19:83:1">83:1</a> O God, do not be silent!
> Do not ignore us! Do not be inactive, O God!
> <a name="19:83:2">83:2</a> For look, your enemies are making a commotion;
> those who hate you are hostile.
> <a name="19:83:3">83:3</a> They carefully plot against your people,
> and make plans to harm the ones you cherish.
> <a name="19:83:4">83:4</a> They say, “Come on, let’s annihilate them so they are no longer a nation!
> Then the name of Israel will be remembered no more.”
> <a name="19:83:5">83:5</a> Yes, they devise a unified strategy;
> they form an alliance against you.
> <a name="19:83:6">83:6</a> It includes the tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites,
> Moab and the Hagrites,
> <a name="19:83:7">83:7</a> Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek,
> Philistia and the inhabitants of Tyre.
> <a name="19:83:8">83:8</a> Even Assyria has allied with them,
> lending its strength to the descendants of Lot. (Selah)
> <a name="19:83:9">83:9</a> Do to them as you did to Midian—
> as you did to Sisera and Jabin at the Kishon River!
> <a name="19:83:10">83:10</a> They were destroyed at Endor;
> their corpses were like manure on the ground.
> <a name="19:83:11">83:11</a> Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb,
> and all their rulers like Zebah and Zalmunna,
> <a name="19:83:12">83:12</a> who said, “Let’s take over the pastures of God!”
> <a name="19:83:13">83:13</a> O my God, make them like dead thistles,
> like dead weeds blown away by the wind!
> <a name="19:83:14">83:14</a> Like the fire that burns down the forest,
> or the flames that consume the mountainsides,
> <a name="19:83:15">83:15</a> chase them with your gale winds,
> and terrify them with your windstorm.
> <a name="19:83:16">83:16</a> Cover their faces with shame,
> so they might seek you, O Lord.
> <a name="19:83:17">83:17</a> May they be humiliated and continually terrified!
> May they die in shame!
> <a name="19:83:18">83:18</a> Then they will know that you alone are the Lord,
> the sovereign king over all the earth.

### Psalm 84

For the music director; according to the gittith style; written by the Korahites, a psalm.

> <a name="19:84:1">84:1</a> How lovely is the place where you live,
> O sovereign Lord!
> <a name="19:84:2">84:2</a> I desperately want to be
> in the courts of the Lord’s temple.
> My heart and my entire being shout for joy
> to the living God.
> <a name="19:84:3">84:3</a> Even the birds find a home there,
> and the swallow builds a nest,
> where she can protect her young
> near your altars, O sovereign Lord,
> my king and my God.
> <a name="19:84:4">84:4</a> How happy are those who live in your temple
> and praise you continually! (Selah)
> <a name="19:84:5">84:5</a> How happy are those who find their strength in you,
> and long to travel the roads that lead to your temple!
> <a name="19:84:6">84:6</a> As they pass through the Baca Valley,
> he provides a spring for them.
> The rain even covers it with pools of water.
> <a name="19:84:7">84:7</a> They are sustained as they travel along;
> each one appears before God in Zion.
> <a name="19:84:8">84:8</a> O Lord, sovereign God,
> hear my prayer!
> Listen, O God of Jacob! (Selah)
> <a name="19:84:9">84:9</a> O God, take notice of our shield!
> Show concern for your chosen king!
> <a name="19:84:10">84:10</a> Certainly spending just one day in your temple courts is better
> than spending a thousand elsewhere.
> I would rather stand at the entrance to the temple of my God
> than live in the tents of the wicked.
> <a name="19:84:11">84:11</a> For the Lord God is our sovereign protector.
> The Lord bestows favor and honor;
> he withholds no good thing from those who have integrity.
> <a name="19:84:12">84:12</a> O sovereign Lord,
> how happy are those who trust in you!

### Psalm 85

For the music director; written by the Korahites, a psalm.

> <a name="19:85:1">85:1</a> O Lord, you showed favor to your land;
> you restored the well-being of Jacob.
> <a name="19:85:2">85:2</a> You pardoned the wrongdoing of your people;
> you forgave all their sin. (Selah)
> <a name="19:85:3">85:3</a> You withdrew all your fury;
> you turned back from your raging anger.
> <a name="19:85:4">85:4</a> Restore us, O God our deliverer!
> Do not be displeased with us!
> <a name="19:85:5">85:5</a> Will you stay mad at us forever?
> Will you remain angry throughout future generations?
> <a name="19:85:6">85:6</a> Will you not revive us once more?
> Then your people will rejoice in you!
> <a name="19:85:7">85:7</a> O Lord, show us your loyal love!
> Bestow on us your deliverance!
> <a name="19:85:8">85:8</a> I will listen to what God the Lord says.
> For he will make peace with his people, his faithful followers.
> Yet they must not return to their foolish ways.
> <a name="19:85:9">85:9</a> Certainly his loyal followers will soon experience his deliverance;
> then his splendor will again appear in our land.
> <a name="19:85:10">85:10</a> Loyal love and faithfulness meet;
> deliverance and peace greet each other with a kiss.
> <a name="19:85:11">85:11</a> Faithfulness grows from the ground,
> and deliverance looks down from the sky.
> <a name="19:85:12">85:12</a> Yes, the Lord will bestow his good blessings,
> and our land will yield its crops.
> <a name="19:85:13">85:13</a> Deliverance goes before him,
> and prepares a pathway for him.

### Psalm 86

A prayer of David.

> <a name="19:86:1">86:1</a> Listen O Lord! Answer me!
> For I am oppressed and needy.
> <a name="19:86:2">86:2</a> Protect me, for I am loyal!
> O my God, deliver your servant, who trusts in you!
> <a name="19:86:3">86:3</a> Have mercy on me, O sovereign Master,
> for I cry out to you all day long!
> <a name="19:86:4">86:4</a> Make your servant glad,
> for to you, O sovereign Master, I pray!
> <a name="19:86:5">86:5</a> Certainly O sovereign Master, you are kind and forgiving,
> and show great faithfulness to all who cry out to you.
> <a name="19:86:6">86:6</a> O Lord, hear my prayer!
> Pay attention to my plea for mercy!
> <a name="19:86:7">86:7</a> In my time of trouble I cry out to you,
> for you will answer me.
> <a name="19:86:8">86:8</a> None can compare to you among the gods, O sovereign Master!
> Your exploits are incomparable!
> <a name="19:86:9">86:9</a> All the nations, whom you created,
> will come and worship you, O sovereign Master.
> They will honor your name.
> <a name="19:86:10">86:10</a> For you are great and do amazing things.
> You alone are God.
> <a name="19:86:11">86:11</a> O Lord, teach me how you want me to live!
> Then I will obey your commands.
> Make me wholeheartedly committed to you!
> <a name="19:86:12">86:12</a> O sovereign Master, my God, I will give you thanks with my whole heart!
> I will honor your name continually!
> <a name="19:86:13">86:13</a> For you will extend your great loyal love to me,
> and will deliver my life from the depths of Sheol.
> <a name="19:86:14">86:14</a> O God, arrogant men attack me;
> a gang of ruthless men, who do not respect you, seek my life.
> <a name="19:86:15">86:15</a> But you, O sovereign Master, are a compassionate and merciful God.
> You are patient and demonstrate great loyal love and faithfulness.
> <a name="19:86:16">86:16</a> Turn toward me and have mercy on me!
> Give your servant your strength!
> Deliver your slave!
> <a name="19:86:17">86:17</a> Show me evidence of your favor!
> Then those who hate me will see it and be ashamed,
> for you, O Lord, will help me and comfort me.

### Psalm 87

Written by the Korahites; a psalm, a song.

> <a name="19:87:1">87:1</a> The Lord’s city is in the holy hills.
> <a name="19:87:2">87:2</a> The Lord loves the gates of Zion
> more than all the dwelling places of Jacob.
> <a name="19:87:3">87:3</a> People say wonderful things about you,
> O city of God. (Selah)
> <a name="19:87:4">87:4</a> I mention Rahab and Babylon to my followers.
> Here are Philistia and Tyre, along with Ethiopia.
> It is said of them, “This one was born there.”
> <a name="19:87:5">87:5</a> But it is said of Zion’s residents,
> “Each one of these was born in her,
> and the Sovereign One makes her secure.”
> <a name="19:87:6">87:6</a> The Lord writes in the census book of the nations,
> “This one was born there.” (Selah)
> <a name="19:87:7">87:7</a> As for the singers, as well as the pipers—
> all of them sing within your walls.

### Psalm 88

A song, a psalm written by the Korahites; for the music director; according to the machalath-leannoth style; a well-written song by Heman the Ezrachite.

> <a name="19:88:1">88:1</a> O Lord God who delivers me!
> By day I cry out
> and at night I pray before you.
> <a name="19:88:2">88:2</a> Listen to my prayer!
> Pay attention to my cry for help!
> <a name="19:88:3">88:3</a> For my life is filled with troubles
> and I am ready to enter Sheol.
> <a name="19:88:4">88:4</a> They treat me like those who descend into the grave.
> I am like a helpless man,
> <a name="19:88:5">88:5</a> adrift among the dead,
> like corpses lying in the grave,
> whom you remember no more,
> and who are cut off from your power.
> <a name="19:88:6">88:6</a> You place me in the lowest regions of the pit,
> in the dark places, in the watery depths.
> <a name="19:88:7">88:7</a> Your anger bears down on me,
> and you overwhelm me with all your waves. (Selah)
> <a name="19:88:8">88:8</a> You cause those who know me to keep their distance;
> you make me an appalling sight to them.
> I am trapped and cannot get free.
> <a name="19:88:9">88:9</a> My eyes grow weak because of oppression.
> I call out to you, O Lord, all day long;
> I spread out my hands in prayer to you.
> <a name="19:88:10">88:10</a> Do you accomplish amazing things for the dead?
> Do the departed spirits rise up and give you thanks? (Selah)
> <a name="19:88:11">88:11</a> Is your loyal love proclaimed in the grave,
> or your faithfulness in the place of the dead?
> <a name="19:88:12">88:12</a> Are your amazing deeds experienced in the dark region,
> or your deliverance in the land of oblivion?
> <a name="19:88:13">88:13</a> As for me, I cry out to you, O Lord;
> in the morning my prayer confronts you.
> <a name="19:88:14">88:14</a> O Lord, why do you reject me,
> and pay no attention to me?
> <a name="19:88:15">88:15</a> I am oppressed and have been on the verge of death since my youth.
> I have been subjected to your horrors and am numb with pain.
> <a name="19:88:16">88:16</a> Your anger overwhelms me;
> your terrors destroy me.
> <a name="19:88:17">88:17</a> They surround me like water all day long;
> they join forces and encircle me.
> <a name="19:88:18">88:18</a> You cause my friends and neighbors to keep their distance;
> those who know me leave me alone in the darkness.

### Psalm 89

A well-written song by Ethan the Ezrachite.

> <a name="19:89:1">89:1</a> I will sing continually about the Lord’s faithful deeds;
> to future generations I will proclaim your faithfulness.
> <a name="19:89:2">89:2</a> For I say, “Loyal love is permanently established;
> in the skies you set up your faithfulness.”
> <a name="19:89:3">89:3</a> The Lord said,
> “I have made a covenant with my chosen one;
> I have made a promise on oath to David, my servant:
> <a name="19:89:4">89:4</a> ‘I will give you an eternal dynasty
> and establish your throne throughout future generations.’” (Selah)
> <a name="19:89:5">89:5</a> O Lord, the heavens praise your amazing deeds,
> as well your faithfulness in the angelic assembly.
> <a name="19:89:6">89:6</a> For who in the skies can compare to the Lord?
> Who is like the Lord among the supernatural beings,
> <a name="19:89:7">89:7</a> a God who is honored in the great angelic assembly,
> and more awesome than all who surround him?
> <a name="19:89:8">89:8</a> O Lord, sovereign God!
> Who is strong like you, O Lord?
> Your faithfulness surrounds you.
> <a name="19:89:9">89:9</a> You rule over the proud sea.
> When its waves surge, you calm them.
> <a name="19:89:10">89:10</a> You crushed the Proud One and killed it;
> with your strong arm you scattered your enemies.
> <a name="19:89:11">89:11</a> The heavens belong to you, as does the earth.
> You made the world and all it contains.
> <a name="19:89:12">89:12</a> You created the north and the south.
> Tabor and Hermon rejoice in your name.
> <a name="19:89:13">89:13</a> Your arm is powerful,
> your hand strong,
> your right hand victorious.
> <a name="19:89:14">89:14</a> Equity and justice are the foundation of your throne.
> Loyal love and faithfulness characterize your rule.
> <a name="19:89:15">89:15</a> How happy are the people who worship you!
> O Lord, they experience your favor.
> <a name="19:89:16">89:16</a> They rejoice in your name all day long,
> and are vindicated by your justice.
> <a name="19:89:17">89:17</a> For you give them splendor and strength.
> By your favor we are victorious.
> <a name="19:89:18">89:18</a> For our shield belongs to the Lord,
> our king to the sovereign Ruler of Israel.
> <a name="19:89:19">89:19</a> Then you spoke through a vision to your faithful followers and said:
> “I have energized a warrior;
> I have raised up a young man from the people.
> <a name="19:89:20">89:20</a> I have discovered David, my servant.
> With my holy oil I have anointed him as king.
> <a name="19:89:21">89:21</a> My hand will support him,
> and my arm will strengthen him.
> <a name="19:89:22">89:22</a> No enemy will be able to exact tribute from him;
> a violent oppressor will not be able to humiliate him.
> <a name="19:89:23">89:23</a> I will crush his enemies before him;
> I will strike down those who hate him.
> <a name="19:89:24">89:24</a> He will experience my faithfulness and loyal love,
> and by my name he will win victories.
> <a name="19:89:25">89:25</a> I will place his hand over the sea,
> his right hand over the rivers.
> <a name="19:89:26">89:26</a> He will call out to me,
> ‘You are my father, my God, and the protector who delivers me.’
> <a name="19:89:27">89:27</a> I will appoint him to be my firstborn son,
> the most exalted of the earth’s kings.
> <a name="19:89:28">89:28</a> I will always extend my loyal love to him,
> and my covenant with him is secure.
> <a name="19:89:29">89:29</a> I will give him an eternal dynasty,
> and make his throne as enduring as the skies above.
> <a name="19:89:30">89:30</a> If his sons reject my law
> and disobey my regulations,
> <a name="19:89:31">89:31</a> if they break my rules
> and do not keep my commandments,
> <a name="19:89:32">89:32</a> I will punish their rebellion by beating them with a club,
> their sin by inflicting them with bruises.
> <a name="19:89:33">89:33</a> But I will not remove my loyal love from him,
> nor be unfaithful to my promise.
> <a name="19:89:34">89:34</a> I will not break my covenant
> or go back on what I promised.
> <a name="19:89:35">89:35</a> Once and for all I have vowed by my own holiness,
> I will never deceive David.
> <a name="19:89:36">89:36</a> His dynasty will last forever.
> His throne will endure before me, like the sun,
> <a name="19:89:37">89:37</a> it will remain stable, like the moon,
> his throne will endure like the skies.” (Selah)
> <a name="19:89:38">89:38</a> But you have spurned and rejected him;
> you are angry with your chosen king.
> <a name="19:89:39">89:39</a> You have repudiated your covenant with your servant;
> you have thrown his crown to the ground.
> <a name="19:89:40">89:40</a> You have broken down all his walls;
> you have made his strongholds a heap of ruins.
> <a name="19:89:41">89:41</a> All who pass by have robbed him;
> he has become an object of disdain to his neighbors.
> <a name="19:89:42">89:42</a> You have allowed his adversaries to be victorious,
> and all his enemies to rejoice.
> <a name="19:89:43">89:43</a> You turn back his sword from the adversary,
> and have not sustained him in battle.
> <a name="19:89:44">89:44</a> You have brought to an end his splendor,
> and have knocked his throne to the ground.
> <a name="19:89:45">89:45</a> You have cut short his youth,
> and have covered him with shame. (Selah)
> <a name="19:89:46">89:46</a> How long, O Lord, will this last?
> Will you remain hidden forever?
> Will your anger continue to burn like fire?
> <a name="19:89:47">89:47</a> Take note of my brief lifespan!
> Why do you make all people so mortal?
> <a name="19:89:48">89:48</a> No man can live on without experiencing death,
> or deliver his life from the power of Sheol. (Selah)
> <a name="19:89:49">89:49</a> Where are your earlier faithful deeds, O sovereign Master,
> the ones performed in accordance with your reliable oath to David?
> <a name="19:89:50">89:50</a> Take note, O sovereign Master, of the way your servants are taunted,
> and of how I must bear so many insults from people!
> <a name="19:89:51">89:51</a> Your enemies, O Lord, hurl insults;
> they insult your chosen king as they dog his footsteps.
> <a name="19:89:52">89:52</a> The Lord deserves praise forevermore!
> We agree! We agree!

## Book 4 (Psalm 90–106)

### Psalm 90

A prayer of Moses, the man of God.

> <a name="19:90:1">90:1</a> O sovereign Master, you have been our protector through all generations!
> <a name="19:90:2">90:2</a> Even before the mountains came into existence,
> or you brought the world into being,
> you were the eternal God.
> <a name="19:90:3">90:3</a> You make mankind return to the dust,
> and say, “Return, O people!”
> <a name="19:90:4">90:4</a> Yes, in your eyes a thousand years
> are like yesterday that quickly passes,
> or like one of the divisions of the nighttime.
> <a name="19:90:5">90:5</a> You bring their lives to an end and they “fall asleep.”
> In the morning they are like the grass that sprouts up;
> <a name="19:90:6">90:6</a> in the morning it glistens and sprouts up;
> at evening time it withers and dries up.
> <a name="19:90:7">90:7</a> Yes, we are consumed by your anger;
> we are terrified by your wrath.
> <a name="19:90:8">90:8</a> You are aware of our sins;
> you even know about our hidden sins.
> <a name="19:90:9">90:9</a> Yes, throughout all our days we experience your raging fury;
> the years of our lives pass quickly, like a sigh.
> <a name="19:90:10">90:10</a> The days of our lives add up to seventy years,
> or eighty, if one is especially strong.
> But even one’s best years are marred by trouble and oppression.
> Yes, they pass quickly and we fly away.
> <a name="19:90:11">90:11</a> Who can really fathom the intensity of your anger?
> Your raging fury causes people to fear you.
> <a name="19:90:12">90:12</a> So teach us to consider our mortality,
> so that we might live wisely.
> <a name="19:90:13">90:13</a> Turn back toward us, O Lord!
> How long must this suffering last?
> Have pity on your servants!
> <a name="19:90:14">90:14</a> Satisfy us in the morning with your loyal love!
> Then we will shout for joy and be happy all our days!
> <a name="19:90:15">90:15</a> Make us happy in proportion to the days you have afflicted us,
> in proportion to the years we have experienced trouble!
> <a name="19:90:16">90:16</a> May your servants see your work!
> May their sons see your majesty!
> <a name="19:90:17">90:17</a> May our sovereign God extend his favor to us!
> Make our endeavors successful!
> Yes, make them successful!

### Psalm 91

> <a name="19:91:1">91:1</a> As for you, the one who lives in the shelter of the Sovereign One,
> and resides in the protective shadow of the mighty king—
> <a name="19:91:2">91:2</a> I say this about the Lord, my shelter and my stronghold,
> my God in whom I trust—
> <a name="19:91:3">91:3</a> he will certainly rescue you from the snare of the hunter
> and from the destructive plague.
> <a name="19:91:4">91:4</a> He will shelter you with his wings;
> you will find safety under his wings.
> His faithfulness is like a shield or a protective wall.
> <a name="19:91:5">91:5</a> You need not fear the terrors of the night,
> the arrow that flies by day,
> <a name="19:91:6">91:6</a> the plague that comes in the darkness,
> or the disease that comes at noon.
> <a name="19:91:7">91:7</a> Though a thousand may fall beside you,
> and a multitude on your right side,
> it will not reach you.
> <a name="19:91:8">91:8</a> Certainly you will see it with your very own eyes—
> you will see the wicked paid back.
> <a name="19:91:9">91:9</a> For you have taken refuge in the Lord,
> my shelter, the Sovereign One.
> <a name="19:91:10">91:10</a> No harm will overtake you;
> no illness will come near your home.
> <a name="19:91:11">91:11</a> For he will order his angels
> to protect you in all you do.
> <a name="19:91:12">91:12</a> They will lift you up in their hands,
> so you will not slip and fall on a stone.
> <a name="19:91:13">91:13</a> You will subdue a lion and a snake;
> you will trample underfoot a young lion and a serpent.
> <a name="19:91:14">91:14</a> The Lord says,
> “Because he is devoted to me, I will deliver him;
> I will protect him because he is loyal to me.
> <a name="19:91:15">91:15</a> When he calls out to me, I will answer him.
> I will be with him when he is in trouble;
> I will rescue him and bring him honor.
> <a name="19:91:16">91:16</a> I will satisfy him with long life,
> and will let him see my salvation.

### Psalm 92

A psalm; a song for the Sabbath day.

> <a name="19:92:1">92:1</a> It is fitting to thank the Lord,
> and to sing praises to your name, O Sovereign One!
> <a name="19:92:2">92:2</a> It is fitting to proclaim your loyal love in the morning,
> and your faithfulness during the night,
> <a name="19:92:3">92:3</a> to the accompaniment of a ten-stringed instrument and a lyre,
> to the accompaniment of the meditative tone of the harp.
> <a name="19:92:4">92:4</a> For you, O Lord, have made me happy by your work.
> I will sing for joy because of what you have done.
> <a name="19:92:5">92:5</a> How great are your works, O Lord!
> Your plans are very intricate!
> <a name="19:92:6">92:6</a> The spiritually insensitive do not recognize this;
> the fool does not understand this.
> <a name="19:92:7">92:7</a> When the wicked sprout up like grass,
> and all the evildoers glisten,
> it is so that they may be annihilated.
> <a name="19:92:8">92:8</a> But you, O Lord, reign forever!
> <a name="19:92:9">92:9</a> Indeed, look at your enemies, O Lord!
> Indeed, look at how your enemies perish!
> All the evildoers are scattered!
> <a name="19:92:10">92:10</a> You exalt my horn like that of a wild ox.
> I am covered with fresh oil.
> <a name="19:92:11">92:11</a> I gloat in triumph over those who tried to ambush me;
> I hear the defeated cries of the evil foes who attacked me.
> <a name="19:92:12">92:12</a> The godly grow like a palm tree;
> they grow high like a cedar in Lebanon.
> <a name="19:92:13">92:13</a> Planted in the Lord’s house,
> they grow in the courts of our God.
> <a name="19:92:14">92:14</a> They bear fruit even when they are old;
> they are filled with vitality and have many leaves.
> <a name="19:92:15">92:15</a> So they proclaim that the Lord, my protector,
> is just and never unfair.

### Psalm 93

> <a name="19:93:1">93:1</a> The Lord reigns!
> He is robed in majesty,
> the Lord is robed,
> he wears strength around his waist.
> Indeed, the world is established, it cannot be moved.
> <a name="19:93:2">93:2</a> Your throne has been secure from ancient times;
> you have always been king.
> <a name="19:93:3">93:3</a> The waves roar, O Lord,
> the waves roar,
> the waves roar and crash.
> <a name="19:93:4">93:4</a> Above the sound of the surging water,
> and the mighty waves of the sea,
> the Lord sits enthroned in majesty.
> <a name="19:93:5">93:5</a> The rules you set down are completely reliable.
> Holiness aptly adorns your house, O Lord, forever.

### Psalm 94

> <a name="19:94:1">94:1</a> O Lord, the God who avenges!
> O God who avenges, reveal your splendor!
> <a name="19:94:2">94:2</a> Rise up, O judge of the earth!
> Pay back the proud!
> <a name="19:94:3">94:3</a> O Lord, how long will the wicked,
> how long will the wicked celebrate?
> <a name="19:94:4">94:4</a> They spew out threats and speak defiantly;
> all the evildoers boast.
> <a name="19:94:5">94:5</a> O Lord, they crush your people;
> they oppress the nation that belongs to you.
> <a name="19:94:6">94:6</a> They kill the widow and the one residing outside his native land,
> and they murder the fatherless.
> <a name="19:94:7">94:7</a> Then they say, “The Lord does not see this;
> the God of Jacob does not take notice of it.”
> <a name="19:94:8">94:8</a> Take notice of this, you ignorant people!
> You fools, when will you ever understand?
> <a name="19:94:9">94:9</a> Does the one who makes the human ear not hear?
> Does the one who forms the human eye not see?
> <a name="19:94:10">94:10</a> Does the one who disciplines the nations not punish?
> He is the one who imparts knowledge to human beings!
> <a name="19:94:11">94:11</a> The Lord knows that
> peoples’ thoughts are morally bankrupt.
> <a name="19:94:12">94:12</a> How happy is the one whom you instruct, O Lord,
> the one whom you teach from your law,
> <a name="19:94:13">94:13</a> in order to protect him from times of trouble,
> until the wicked are destroyed.
> <a name="19:94:14">94:14</a> Certainly the Lord does not forsake his people;
> he does not abandon the nation that belongs to him.
> <a name="19:94:15">94:15</a> For justice will prevail,
> and all the morally upright will be vindicated.
> <a name="19:94:16">94:16</a> Who will rise up to defend me against the wicked?
> Who will stand up for me against the evildoers?
> <a name="19:94:17">94:17</a> If the Lord had not helped me,
> I would have laid down in the silence of death.
> <a name="19:94:18">94:18</a> If I say, “My foot is slipping,”
> your loyal love, O Lord, supports me.
> <a name="19:94:19">94:19</a> When worries threaten to overwhelm me,
> your soothing touch makes me happy.
> <a name="19:94:20">94:20</a> Cruel rulers are not your allies,
> those who make oppressive laws.
> <a name="19:94:21">94:21</a> They conspire against the blameless,
> and condemn to death the innocent.
> <a name="19:94:22">94:22</a> But the Lord will protect me,
> and my God will shelter me.
> <a name="19:94:23">94:23</a> He will pay them back for their sin.
> He will destroy them because of their evil;
> the Lord our God will destroy them.

### Psalm 95

> <a name="19:95:1">95:1</a> Come! Let’s sing for joy to the Lord!
> Let’s shout out praises to our protector who delivers us!
> <a name="19:95:2">95:2</a> Let’s enter his presence with thanksgiving!
> Let’s shout out to him in celebration!
> <a name="19:95:3">95:3</a> For the Lord is a great God,
> a great king who is superior to all gods.
> <a name="19:95:4">95:4</a> The depths of the earth are in his hand,
> and the mountain peaks belong to him.
> <a name="19:95:5">95:5</a> The sea is his, for he made it.
> His hands formed the dry land.
> <a name="19:95:6">95:6</a> Come! Let’s bow down and worship!
> Let’s kneel before the Lord, our creator!
> <a name="19:95:7">95:7</a> For he is our God;
> we are the people of his pasture,
> the sheep he owns.
> Today, if only you would obey him!
> <a name="19:95:8">95:8</a> He says, “Do not be stubborn like they were at Meribah,
> like they were that day at Massah in the wilderness,
> <a name="19:95:9">95:9</a> where your ancestors challenged my authority,
> and tried my patience, even though they had seen my work.
> <a name="19:95:10">95:10</a> For forty years I was continually disgusted with that generation,
> and I said, ‘These people desire to go astray;
> they do not obey my commands.’
> <a name="19:95:11">95:11</a> So I made a vow in my anger,
> ‘They will never enter into the resting place I had set aside for them.’”

### Psalm 96

> <a name="19:96:1">96:1</a> Sing to the Lord a new song!
> Sing to the Lord, all the earth!
> <a name="19:96:2">96:2</a> Sing to the Lord! Praise his name!
> Announce every day how he delivers!
> <a name="19:96:3">96:3</a> Tell the nations about his splendor!
> Tell all the nations about his amazing deeds!
> <a name="19:96:4">96:4</a> For the Lord is great and certainly worthy of praise;
> he is more awesome than all gods.
> <a name="19:96:5">96:5</a> For all the gods of the nations are worthless,
> but the Lord made the sky.
> <a name="19:96:6">96:6</a> Majestic splendor emanates from him;
> his sanctuary is firmly established and beautiful.
> <a name="19:96:7">96:7</a> Ascribe to the Lord, O families of the nations,
> ascribe to the Lord splendor and strength!
> <a name="19:96:8">96:8</a> Ascribe to the Lord the splendor he deserves!
> Bring an offering and enter his courts!
> <a name="19:96:9">96:9</a> Worship the Lord in holy attire!
> Tremble before him, all the earth!
> <a name="19:96:10">96:10</a> Say among the nations, “The Lord reigns!
> The world is established, it cannot be moved.
> He judges the nations fairly.”
> <a name="19:96:11">96:11</a> Let the sky rejoice, and the earth be happy!
> Let the sea and everything in it shout!
> <a name="19:96:12">96:12</a> Let the fields and everything in them celebrate!
> Then let the trees of the forest shout with joy
> <a name="19:96:13">96:13</a> before the Lord, for he comes!
> For he comes to judge the earth!
> He judges the world fairly,
> and the nations in accordance with his justice.

### Psalm 97

> <a name="19:97:1">97:1</a> The Lord reigns!
> Let the earth be happy!
> Let the many coastlands rejoice!
> <a name="19:97:2">97:2</a> Dark clouds surround him;
> equity and justice are the foundation of his throne.
> <a name="19:97:3">97:3</a> Fire goes before him;
> on every side it burns up his enemies.
> <a name="19:97:4">97:4</a> His lightning bolts light up the world;
> the earth sees and trembles.
> <a name="19:97:5">97:5</a> The mountains melt like wax before the Lord,
> before the sovereign Master of the whole earth.
> <a name="19:97:6">97:6</a> The sky declares his justice,
> and all the nations see his splendor.
> <a name="19:97:7">97:7</a> All who worship idols are ashamed,
> those who boast about worthless idols.
> All the gods bow down before him.
> <a name="19:97:8">97:8</a> Zion hears and rejoices,
> the towns of Judah are happy,
> because of your judgments, O Lord.
> <a name="19:97:9">97:9</a> For you, O Lord, are the sovereign king over the whole earth;
> you are elevated high above all gods.
> <a name="19:97:10">97:10</a> You who love the Lord, hate evil!
> He protects the lives of his faithful followers;
> he delivers them from the power of the wicked.
> <a name="19:97:11">97:11</a> The godly bask in the light;
> the morally upright experience joy.
> <a name="19:97:12">97:12</a> You godly ones, rejoice in the Lord!
> give thanks to his holy name.

### Psalm 98

A psalm.

> <a name="19:98:1">98:1</a> Sing to the Lord a new song,
> for he performs amazing deeds!
> His right hand and his mighty arm
> accomplish deliverance.
> <a name="19:98:2">98:2</a> The Lord demonstrates his power to deliver;
> in the sight of the nations he reveals his justice.
> <a name="19:98:3">98:3</a> He remains loyal and faithful to the family of Israel.
> All the ends of the earth see our God deliver us.
> <a name="19:98:4">98:4</a> Shout out praises to the Lord, all the earth!
> Break out in a joyful shout and sing!
> <a name="19:98:5">98:5</a> Sing to the Lord accompanied by a harp,
> accompanied by a harp and the sound of music!
> <a name="19:98:6">98:6</a> With trumpets and the blaring of the ram’s horn,
> shout out praises before the king, the Lord!
> <a name="19:98:7">98:7</a> Let the sea and everything in it shout,
> along with the world and those who live in it!
> <a name="19:98:8">98:8</a> Let the rivers clap their hands!
> Let the mountains sing in unison
> <a name="19:98:9">98:9</a> before the Lord!
> For he comes to judge the earth!
> He judges the world fairly,
> and the nations in a just manner.

### Psalm 99

> <a name="19:99:1">99:1</a> The Lord reigns!
> The nations tremble.
> He sits enthroned above the winged angels;
> the earth shakes.
> <a name="19:99:2">99:2</a> The Lord is elevated in Zion;
> he is exalted over all the nations.
> <a name="19:99:3">99:3</a> Let them praise your great and awesome name!
> He is holy!
> <a name="19:99:4">99:4</a> The king is strong;
> he loves justice.
> You ensure that legal decisions will be made fairly;
> you promote justice and equity in Jacob.
> <a name="19:99:5">99:5</a> Praise the Lord our God!
> Worship before his footstool!
> He is holy!
> <a name="19:99:6">99:6</a> Moses and Aaron were among his priests;
> Samuel was one of those who prayed to him.
> They prayed to the Lord and he answered them.
> <a name="19:99:7">99:7</a> He spoke to them from a pillar of cloud;
> they obeyed his regulations and the ordinance he gave them.
> <a name="19:99:8">99:8</a> O Lord our God, you answered them.
> They found you to be a forgiving God,
> but also one who punished their sinful deeds.
> <a name="19:99:9">99:9</a> Praise the Lord our God!
> Worship on his holy hill,
> for the Lord our God is holy!

### Psalm 100

A thanksgiving psalm.

> <a name="19:100:1">100:1</a> Shout out praises to the Lord, all the earth!
> <a name="19:100:2">100:2</a> Worship the Lord with joy!
> Enter his presence with joyful singing!
> <a name="19:100:3">100:3</a> Realize that the Lord is God!
> He made us and we belong to him;
> we are his people, the sheep of his pasture.
> <a name="19:100:4">100:4</a> Enter his gates with thanksgiving,
> and his courts with praise!
> Give him thanks!
> Praise his name!
> <a name="19:100:5">100:5</a> For the Lord is good.
> His loyal love endures,
> and he is faithful through all generations.

### Psalm 101

A psalm of David.

> <a name="19:101:1">101:1</a> I will sing about loyalty and justice!
> To you, O Lord, I will sing praises!
> <a name="19:101:2">101:2</a> I will walk in the way of integrity.
> When will you come to me?
> I will conduct my business with integrity in the midst of my palace.
> <a name="19:101:3">101:3</a> I will not even consider doing what is dishonest.
> I hate doing evil;
> I will have no part of it.
> <a name="19:101:4">101:4</a> I will have nothing to do with a perverse person;
> I will not permit evil.
> <a name="19:101:5">101:5</a> I will destroy anyone who slanders his neighbor in secret.
> I will not tolerate anyone who has a cocky demeanor and an arrogant attitude.
> <a name="19:101:6">101:6</a> I will favor the honest people of the land,
> and allow them to live with me.
> Those who walk in the way of integrity will attend me.
> <a name="19:101:7">101:7</a> Deceitful people will not live in my palace.
> Liars will not be welcome in my presence.
> <a name="19:101:8">101:8</a> Each morning I will destroy all the wicked people in the land,
> and remove all evildoers from the city of the Lord.

### Psalm 102

The prayer of an oppressed man, as he grows faint and pours out his lament before the Lord.

> <a name="19:102:1">102:1</a> O Lord, hear my prayer!
> Pay attention to my cry for help!
> <a name="19:102:2">102:2</a> Do not ignore me in my time of trouble!
> Listen to me!
> When I call out to you, quickly answer me!
> <a name="19:102:3">102:3</a> For my days go up in smoke,
> and my bones are charred like a fireplace.
> <a name="19:102:4">102:4</a> My heart is parched and withered like grass,
> for I am unable to eat food.
> <a name="19:102:5">102:5</a> Because of the anxiety that makes me groan,
> my bones protrude from my skin.
> <a name="19:102:6">102:6</a> I am like an owl in the wilderness;
> I am like a screech owl among the ruins.
> <a name="19:102:7">102:7</a> I stay awake;
> I am like a solitary bird on a roof.
> <a name="19:102:8">102:8</a> All day long my enemies taunt me;
> those who mock me use my name in their curses.
> <a name="19:102:9">102:9</a> For I eat ashes as if they were bread,
> and mix my drink with my tears,
> <a name="19:102:10">102:10</a> because of your anger and raging fury.
> Indeed, you pick me up and throw me away.
> <a name="19:102:11">102:11</a> My days are coming to an end,
> and I am withered like grass.
> <a name="19:102:12">102:12</a> But you, O Lord, rule forever,
> and your reputation endures.
> <a name="19:102:13">102:13</a> You will rise up and have compassion on Zion.
> For it is time to have mercy on her,
> for the appointed time has come.
> <a name="19:102:14">102:14</a> Indeed, your servants take delight in her stones,
> and feel compassion for the dust of her ruins.
> <a name="19:102:15">102:15</a> The nations will respect the reputation of the Lord,
> and all the kings of the earth will respect his splendor,
> <a name="19:102:16">102:16</a> when the Lord rebuilds Zion,
> and reveals his splendor,
> <a name="19:102:17">102:17</a> when he responds to the prayer of the destitute,
> and does not reject their request.
> <a name="19:102:18">102:18</a> The account of his intervention will be recorded for future generations;
> people yet to be born will praise the Lord.
> <a name="19:102:19">102:19</a> For he will look down from his sanctuary above;
> from heaven the Lord will look toward earth,
> <a name="19:102:20">102:20</a> in order to hear the painful cries of the prisoners,
> and to set free those condemned to die,
> <a name="19:102:21">102:21</a> so they may proclaim the name of the Lord in Zion,
> and praise him in Jerusalem,
> <a name="19:102:22">102:22</a> when the nations gather together,
> and the kingdoms pay tribute to the Lord.
> <a name="19:102:23">102:23</a> He has taken away my strength in the middle of life;
> he has cut short my days.
> <a name="19:102:24">102:24</a> I say, “O my God, please do not take me away in the middle of my life!
> You endure through all generations.
> <a name="19:102:25">102:25</a> In earlier times you established the earth;
> the skies are your handiwork.
> <a name="19:102:26">102:26</a> They will perish,
> but you will endure.
> They will wear out like a garment;
> like clothes you will remove them and they will disappear.
> <a name="19:102:27">102:27</a> But you remain;
> your years do not come to an end.
> <a name="19:102:28">102:28</a> The children of your servants will settle down here,
> and their descendants will live securely in your presence.”

### Psalm 103

By David.

> <a name="19:103:1">103:1</a> Praise the Lord, O my soul!
> With all that is within me, praise his holy name!
> <a name="19:103:2">103:2</a> Praise the Lord, O my soul!
> Do not forget all his kind deeds!
> <a name="19:103:3">103:3</a> He is the one who forgives all your sins,
> who heals all your diseases,
> <a name="19:103:4">103:4</a> who delivers your life from the Pit,
> who crowns you with his loyal love and compassion,
> <a name="19:103:5">103:5</a> who satisfies your life with good things,
> so your youth is renewed like an eagle’s.
> <a name="19:103:6">103:6</a> The Lord does what is fair,
> and executes justice for all the oppressed.
> <a name="19:103:7">103:7</a> The Lord revealed his faithful acts to Moses,
> his deeds to the Israelites.
> <a name="19:103:8">103:8</a> The Lord is compassionate and merciful;
> he is patient and demonstrates great loyal love.
> <a name="19:103:9">103:9</a> He does not always accuse,
> and does not stay angry.
> <a name="19:103:10">103:10</a> He does not deal with us as our sins deserve;
> he does not repay us as our misdeeds deserve.
> <a name="19:103:11">103:11</a> For as the skies are high above the earth,
> so his loyal love towers over his faithful followers.
> <a name="19:103:12">103:12</a> As far as the eastern horizon is from the west,
> so he removes the guilt of our rebellious actions from us.
> <a name="19:103:13">103:13</a> As a father has compassion on his children,
> so the Lord has compassion on his faithful followers.
> <a name="19:103:14">103:14</a> For he knows what we are made of;
> he realizes we are made of clay.
> <a name="19:103:15">103:15</a> A person’s life is like grass.
> Like a flower in the field it flourishes,
> <a name="19:103:16">103:16</a> but when the hot wind blows by, it disappears,
> and one can no longer even spot the place where it once grew.
> <a name="19:103:17">103:17</a> But the Lord continually shows loyal love to his faithful followers,
> and is faithful to their descendants,
> <a name="19:103:18">103:18</a> to those who keep his covenant,
> who are careful to obey his commands.
> <a name="19:103:19">103:19</a> The Lord has established his throne in heaven;
> his kingdom extends over everything.
> <a name="19:103:20">103:20</a> Praise the Lord, you angels of his,
> you powerful warriors who carry out his decrees
> and obey his orders!
> <a name="19:103:21">103:21</a> Praise the Lord, all you warriors of his,
> you servants of his who carry out his desires!
> <a name="19:103:22">103:22</a> Praise the Lord, all that he has made,
> in all the regions of his kingdom!
> Praise the Lord, O my soul!

### Psalm 104

> <a name="19:104:1">104:1</a> Praise the Lord, O my soul!
> O Lord my God, you are magnificent.
> You are robed in splendor and majesty.
> <a name="19:104:2">104:2</a> He covers himself with light as if it were a garment.
> He stretches out the skies like a tent curtain,
> <a name="19:104:3">104:3</a> and lays the beams of the upper rooms of his palace on the rain clouds.
> He makes the clouds his chariot,
> and travels along on the wings of the wind.
> <a name="19:104:4">104:4</a> He makes the winds his messengers,
> and the flaming fire his attendant.
> <a name="19:104:5">104:5</a> He established the earth on its foundations;
> it will never be upended.
> <a name="19:104:6">104:6</a> The watery deep covered it like a garment;
> the waters reached above the mountains.
> <a name="19:104:7">104:7</a> Your shout made the waters retreat;
> at the sound of your thunderous voice they hurried off—
> <a name="19:104:8">104:8</a> as the mountains rose up,
> and the valleys went down—
> to the place you appointed for them.
> <a name="19:104:9">104:9</a> You set up a boundary for them that they could not cross,
> so that they would not cover the earth again.
> <a name="19:104:10">104:10</a> He turns springs into streams;
> they flow between the mountains.
> <a name="19:104:11">104:11</a> They provide water for all the animals in the field;
> the wild donkeys quench their thirst.
> <a name="19:104:12">104:12</a> The birds of the sky live beside them;
> they chirp among the bushes.
> <a name="19:104:13">104:13</a> He waters the mountains from the upper rooms of his palace;
> the earth is full of the fruit you cause to grow.
> <a name="19:104:14">104:14</a> He provides grass for the cattle,
> and crops for people to cultivate,
> so they can produce food from the ground,
> <a name="19:104:15">104:15</a> as well as wine that makes people feel so good,
> and so they can have oil to make their faces shine,
> as well as food that sustains people’s lives.
> <a name="19:104:16">104:16</a> The trees of the Lord receive all the rain they need,
> the cedars of Lebanon which he planted,
> <a name="19:104:17">104:17</a> where the birds make nests,
> near the evergreens in which the herons live.
> <a name="19:104:18">104:18</a> The wild goats live in the high mountains;
> the rock badgers find safety in the cliffs.
> <a name="19:104:19">104:19</a> He made the moon to mark the months,
> and the sun sets according to a regular schedule.
> <a name="19:104:20">104:20</a> You make it dark and night comes,
> during which all the beasts of the forest prowl around.
> <a name="19:104:21">104:21</a> The lions roar for prey,
> seeking their food from God.
> <a name="19:104:22">104:22</a> When the sun rises, they withdraw
> and sleep in their dens.
> <a name="19:104:23">104:23</a> Men then go out to do their work,
> and labor away until evening.
> <a name="19:104:24">104:24</a> How many living things you have made, O Lord!
> You have exhibited great skill in making all of them;
> the earth is full of the living things you have made.
> <a name="19:104:25">104:25</a> Over here is the deep, wide sea,
> which teems with innumerable swimming creatures,
> living things both small and large.
> <a name="19:104:26">104:26</a> The ships travel there,
> and over here swims the whale you made to play in it.
> <a name="19:104:27">104:27</a> All of your creatures wait for you
> to provide them with food on a regular basis.
> <a name="19:104:28">104:28</a> You give food to them and they receive it;
> you open your hand and they are filled with food.
> <a name="19:104:29">104:29</a> When you ignore them, they panic.
> When you take away their life’s breath, they die
> and return to dust.
> <a name="19:104:30">104:30</a> When you send your life-giving breath, they are created,
> and you replenish the surface of the ground.
> <a name="19:104:31">104:31</a> May the splendor of the Lord endure!
> May the Lord find pleasure in the living things he has made!
> <a name="19:104:32">104:32</a> He looks down on the earth and it shakes;
> he touches the mountains and they start to smolder.
> <a name="19:104:33">104:33</a> I will sing to the Lord as long as I live;
> I will sing praise to my God as long as I exist!
> <a name="19:104:34">104:34</a> May my thoughts be pleasing to him!
> I will rejoice in the Lord.
> <a name="19:104:35">104:35</a> May sinners disappear from the earth,
> and the wicked vanish!
> Praise the Lord, O my soul!
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 105

> <a name="19:105:1">105:1</a> Give thanks to the Lord!
> Call on his name!
> Make known his accomplishments among the nations!
> <a name="19:105:2">105:2</a> Sing to him!
> Make music to him!
> Reflect on all his miraculous deeds!
> <a name="19:105:3">105:3</a> Boast about his holy name!
> Let the hearts of those who seek the Lord rejoice!
> <a name="19:105:4">105:4</a> Seek the Lord and the strength he gives!
> Seek his presence continually!
> <a name="19:105:5">105:5</a> Recall the miraculous deeds he performed,
> his mighty acts and the judgments he decreed,
> <a name="19:105:6">105:6</a> O children of Abraham, his servant,
> you descendants of Jacob, his chosen ones!
> <a name="19:105:7">105:7</a> He is the Lord our God;
> he carries out judgment throughout the earth.
> <a name="19:105:8">105:8</a> He always remembers his covenantal decree,
> the promise he made to a thousand generations—
> <a name="19:105:9">105:9</a> the one he made to Abraham,
> the promise he made by oath to Isaac!
> <a name="19:105:10">105:10</a> He gave it to Jacob as a decree,
> to Israel as a lasting promise,
> <a name="19:105:11">105:11</a> saying, “To you I will give the land of Canaan
> as the portion of your inheritance.”
> <a name="19:105:12">105:12</a> When they were few in number,
> just a very few, and resident aliens within it,
> <a name="19:105:13">105:13</a> they wandered from nation to nation,
> and from one kingdom to another.
> <a name="19:105:14">105:14</a> He let no one oppress them;
> he disciplined kings for their sake,
> <a name="19:105:15">105:15</a> saying,“Don’t touch my chosen ones!
> Don’t harm my prophets!”
> <a name="19:105:16">105:16</a> He called down a famine upon the earth;
> he cut off all the food supply.
> <a name="19:105:17">105:17</a> He sent a man ahead of them—
> Joseph was sold as a servant.
> <a name="19:105:18">105:18</a> The shackles hurt his feet;
> his neck was placed in an iron collar,
> <a name="19:105:19">105:19</a> until the time when his prediction came true.
> The Lord’s word proved him right.
> <a name="19:105:20">105:20</a> The king authorized his release;
> the ruler of nations set him free.
> <a name="19:105:21">105:21</a> He put him in charge of his palace,
> and made him manager of all his property,
> <a name="19:105:22">105:22</a> giving him authority to imprison his officials
> and to teach his advisers.
> <a name="19:105:23">105:23</a> Israel moved to Egypt;
> Jacob lived for a time in the land of Ham.
> <a name="19:105:24">105:24</a> The Lord made his people very fruitful,
> and made them more numerous than their enemies.
> <a name="19:105:25">105:25</a> He caused them to hate his people,
> and to mistreat his servants.
> <a name="19:105:26">105:26</a> He sent his servant Moses,
> and Aaron, whom he had chosen.
> <a name="19:105:27">105:27</a> They executed his miraculous signs among them,
> and his amazing deeds in the land of Ham.
> <a name="19:105:28">105:28</a> He made it dark;
> they did not disobey his orders.
> <a name="19:105:29">105:29</a> He turned their water into blood,
> and killed their fish.
> <a name="19:105:30">105:30</a> Their land was overrun by frogs,
> which even got into the rooms of their kings.
> <a name="19:105:31">105:31</a> He ordered flies to come;
> gnats invaded their whole territory.
> <a name="19:105:32">105:32</a> He sent hail along with the rain;
> there was lightning in their land.
> <a name="19:105:33">105:33</a> He destroyed their vines and fig trees,
> and broke the trees throughout their territory.
> <a name="19:105:34">105:34</a> He ordered locusts to come,
> innumerable grasshoppers.
> <a name="19:105:35">105:35</a> They ate all the vegetation in their land,
> and devoured the crops of their fields.
> <a name="19:105:36">105:36</a> He struck down all the firstborn in their land,
> the firstfruits of their reproductive power.
> <a name="19:105:37">105:37</a> He brought his people out enriched with silver and gold;
> none of his tribes stumbled.
> <a name="19:105:38">105:38</a> Egypt was happy when they left,
> for they were afraid of them.
> <a name="19:105:39">105:39</a> He spread out a cloud for a cover,
> and provided a fire to light up the night.
> <a name="19:105:40">105:40</a> They asked for food, and he sent quails;
> he satisfied them with food from the sky.
> <a name="19:105:41">105:41</a> He opened up a rock and water flowed out;
> a river ran through dry regions.
> <a name="19:105:42">105:42</a> Yes, he remembered the sacred promise
> he made to Abraham his servant.
> <a name="19:105:43">105:43</a> When he led his people out, they rejoiced;
> his chosen ones shouted with joy.
> <a name="19:105:44">105:44</a> He handed the territory of nations over to them,
> and they took possession of what other peoples had produced,
> <a name="19:105:45">105:45</a> so that they might keep his commands
> and obey his laws.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 106

> <a name="19:106:1">106:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Give thanks to the Lord, for he is good,
> and his loyal love endures!
> <a name="19:106:2">106:2</a> Who can adequately recount the Lord’s mighty acts,
> or relate all his praiseworthy deeds?
> <a name="19:106:3">106:3</a> How happy are those who promote justice,
> and do what is right all the time!
> <a name="19:106:4">106:4</a> Remember me, O Lord, when you show favor to your people!
> Pay attention to me, when you deliver,
> <a name="19:106:5">106:5</a> so I may see the prosperity of your chosen ones,
> rejoice along with your nation,
> and boast along with the people who belong to you.
> <a name="19:106:6">106:6</a> We have sinned like our ancestors;
> we have done wrong, we have done evil.
> <a name="19:106:7">106:7</a> Our ancestors in Egypt failed to appreciate your miraculous deeds,
> they failed to remember your many acts of loyal love,
> and they rebelled at the sea, by the Red Sea.
> <a name="19:106:8">106:8</a> Yet he delivered them for the sake of his reputation,
> that he might reveal his power.
> <a name="19:106:9">106:9</a> He shouted at the Red Sea and it dried up;
> he led them through the deep water as if it were a desert.
> <a name="19:106:10">106:10</a> He delivered them from the power of the one who hated them,
> and rescued them from the power of the enemy.
> <a name="19:106:11">106:11</a> The water covered their enemies;
> not even one of them survived.
> <a name="19:106:12">106:12</a> They believed his promises;
> they sang praises to him.
> <a name="19:106:13">106:13</a> They quickly forgot what he had done;
> they did not wait for his instructions.
> <a name="19:106:14">106:14</a> In the wilderness they had an insatiable craving for meat;
> they challenged God in the desert.
> <a name="19:106:15">106:15</a> He granted their request,
> then struck them with a disease.
> <a name="19:106:16">106:16</a> In the camp they resented Moses,
> and Aaron, the Lord’s holy priest.
> <a name="19:106:17">106:17</a> The earth opened up and swallowed Dathan;
> it engulfed the group led by Abiram.
> <a name="19:106:18">106:18</a> Fire burned their group;
> the flames scorched the wicked.
> <a name="19:106:19">106:19</a> They made an image of a calf at Horeb,
> and worshiped a metal idol.
> <a name="19:106:20">106:20</a> They traded their majestic God
> for the image of an ox that eats grass.
> <a name="19:106:21">106:21</a> They rejected the God who delivered them,
> the one who performed great deeds in Egypt,
> <a name="19:106:22">106:22</a> amazing feats in the land of Ham,
> mighty acts by the Red Sea.
> <a name="19:106:23">106:23</a> He threatened to destroy them,
> but Moses, his chosen one, interceded with him
> and turned back his destructive anger.
> <a name="19:106:24">106:24</a> They rejected the fruitful land;
> they did not believe his promise.
> <a name="19:106:25">106:25</a> They grumbled in their tents;
> they did not obey the Lord.
> <a name="19:106:26">106:26</a> So he made a solemn vow
> that he would make them die in the desert,
> <a name="19:106:27">106:27</a> make their descendants die among the nations,
> and scatter them among foreign lands.
> <a name="19:106:28">106:28</a> They worshiped Baal of Peor,
> and ate sacrifices offered to the dead.
> <a name="19:106:29">106:29</a> They made the Lord angry by their actions,
> and a plague broke out among them.
> <a name="19:106:30">106:30</a> Phinehas took a stand and intervened,
> and the plague subsided.
> <a name="19:106:31">106:31</a> This brought him a reward,
> an eternal gift.
> <a name="19:106:32">106:32</a> They made him angry by the waters of Meribah,
> and Moses suffered because of them,
> <a name="19:106:33">106:33</a> for they aroused his temper,
> and he spoke rashly.
> <a name="19:106:34">106:34</a> They did not destroy the nations,
> as the Lord had commanded them to do.
> <a name="19:106:35">106:35</a> They mixed in with the nations
> and learned their ways.
> <a name="19:106:36">106:36</a> They worshiped their idols,
> which became a snare to them.
> <a name="19:106:37">106:37</a> They sacrificed their sons and daughters to demons.
> <a name="19:106:38">106:38</a> They shed innocent blood—
> the blood of their sons and daughters,
> whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan.
> The land was polluted by bloodshed.
> <a name="19:106:39">106:39</a> They were defiled by their deeds,
> and unfaithful in their actions.
> <a name="19:106:40">106:40</a> So the Lord was angry with his people
> and despised the people who belong to him.
> <a name="19:106:41">106:41</a> He handed them over to the nations,
> and those who hated them ruled over them.
> <a name="19:106:42">106:42</a> Their enemies oppressed them;
> they were subject to their authority.
> <a name="19:106:43">106:43</a> Many times he delivered them,
> but they had a rebellious attitude,
> and degraded themselves by their sin.
> <a name="19:106:44">106:44</a> Yet he took notice of their distress,
> when he heard their cry for help.
> <a name="19:106:45">106:45</a> He remembered his covenant with them,
> and relented because of his great loyal love.
> <a name="19:106:46">106:46</a> He caused all their conquerors
> to have pity on them.
> <a name="19:106:47">106:47</a> Deliver us, O Lord, our God!
> Gather us from among the nations!
> Then we will give thanks to your holy name,
> and boast about your praiseworthy deeds.
> <a name="19:106:48">106:48</a> The Lord God of Israel deserves praise,
> in the future and forevermore.
> Let all the people say, “We agree! Praise the Lord!”

## Book 5 (107–150)

### Psalm 107

> <a name="19:107:1">107:1</a> Give thanks to the Lord, for he is good,
> and his loyal love endures!
> <a name="19:107:2">107:2</a> Let those delivered by the Lord speak out,
> those whom he delivered from the power of the enemy,
> <a name="19:107:3">107:3</a> and gathered from foreign lands,
> from east and west,
> from north and south.
> <a name="19:107:4">107:4</a> They wandered through the wilderness on a desert road;
> they found no city in which to live.
> <a name="19:107:5">107:5</a> They were hungry and thirsty;
> they fainted from exhaustion.
> <a name="19:107:6">107:6</a> They cried out to the Lord in their distress;
> he delivered them from their troubles.
> <a name="19:107:7">107:7</a> He led them on a level road,
> that they might find a city in which to live.
> <a name="19:107:8">107:8</a> Let them give thanks to the Lord for his loyal love,
> and for the amazing things he has done for people!
> <a name="19:107:9">107:9</a> For he has satisfied those who thirst,
> and those who hunger he has filled with food.
> <a name="19:107:10">107:10</a> They sat in utter darkness,
> bound in painful iron chains,
> <a name="19:107:11">107:11</a> because they had rebelled against God’s commands,
> and rejected the instructions of the sovereign king.
> <a name="19:107:12">107:12</a> So he used suffering to humble them;
> they stumbled and no one helped them up.
> <a name="19:107:13">107:13</a> They cried out to the Lord in their distress;
> he delivered them from their troubles.
> <a name="19:107:14">107:14</a> He brought them out of the utter darkness,
> and tore off their shackles.
> <a name="19:107:15">107:15</a> Let them give thanks to the Lord for his loyal love,
> and for the amazing things he has done for people!
> <a name="19:107:16">107:16</a> For he shattered the bronze gates,
> and hacked through the iron bars.
> <a name="19:107:17">107:17</a> They acted like fools in their rebellious ways,
> and suffered because of their sins.
> <a name="19:107:18">107:18</a> They lost their appetite for all food,
> and they drew near the gates of death.
> <a name="19:107:19">107:19</a> They cried out to the Lord in their distress;
> he delivered them from their troubles.
> <a name="19:107:20">107:20</a> He sent them an assuring word and healed them;
> he rescued them from the pits where they were trapped.
> <a name="19:107:21">107:21</a> Let them give thanks to the Lord for his loyal love,
> and for the amazing things he has done for people!
> <a name="19:107:22">107:22</a> Let them present thank offerings,
> and loudly proclaim what he has done!
> <a name="19:107:23">107:23</a> Some traveled on the sea in ships,
> and carried cargo over the vast waters.
> <a name="19:107:24">107:24</a> They witnessed the acts of the Lord,
> his amazing feats on the deep water.
> <a name="19:107:25">107:25</a> He gave the order for a windstorm,
> and it stirred up the waves of the sea.
> <a name="19:107:26">107:26</a> They reached up to the sky,
> then dropped into the depths.
> The sailors’ strength left them because the danger was so great.
> <a name="19:107:27">107:27</a> They swayed and staggered like a drunk,
> and all their skill proved ineffective.
> <a name="19:107:28">107:28</a> They cried out to the Lord in their distress;
> he delivered them from their troubles.
> <a name="19:107:29">107:29</a> He calmed the storm,
> and the waves grew silent.
> <a name="19:107:30">107:30</a> The sailors rejoiced because the waves grew quiet,
> and he led them to the harbor they desired.
> <a name="19:107:31">107:31</a> Let them give thanks to the Lord for his loyal love,
> and for the amazing things he has done for people!
> <a name="19:107:32">107:32</a> Let them exalt him in the assembly of the people!
> Let them praise him in the place where the leaders preside!
> <a name="19:107:33">107:33</a> He turned streams into a desert,
> springs of water into arid land,
> <a name="19:107:34">107:34</a> and a fruitful land into a barren place,
> because of the sin of its inhabitants.
> <a name="19:107:35">107:35</a> As for his people, he turned a desert into a pool of water,
> and a dry land into springs of water.
> <a name="19:107:36">107:36</a> He allowed the hungry to settle there,
> and they established a city in which to live.
> <a name="19:107:37">107:37</a> They cultivated fields,
> and planted vineyards,
> which yielded a harvest of fruit.
> <a name="19:107:38">107:38</a> He blessed them so that they became very numerous.
> He would not allow their cattle to decrease in number.
> <a name="19:107:39">107:39</a> As for their enemies, they decreased in number and were beaten down,
> because of painful distress and suffering.
> <a name="19:107:40">107:40</a> He would pour contempt upon princes,
> and he made them wander in a wasteland with no road.
> <a name="19:107:41">107:41</a> Yet he protected the needy from oppression,
> and cared for his families like a flock of sheep.
> <a name="19:107:42">107:42</a> When the godly see this, they rejoice,
> and every sinner shuts his mouth.
> <a name="19:107:43">107:43</a> Whoever is wise, let him take note of these things!
> Let them consider the Lord’s acts of loyal love!

### Psalm 108

A song, a psalm of David.

> <a name="19:108:1">108:1</a> I am determined, O God!
> I will sing and praise you with my whole heart.
> <a name="19:108:2">108:2</a> Awake, O stringed instrument and harp!
> I will wake up at dawn!
> <a name="19:108:3">108:3</a> I will give you thanks before the nations, O Lord!
> I will sing praises to you before foreigners!
> <a name="19:108:4">108:4</a> For your loyal love extends beyond the sky,
> and your faithfulness reaches the clouds.
> <a name="19:108:5">108:5</a> Rise up above the sky, O God!
> May your splendor cover the whole earth!
> <a name="19:108:6">108:6</a> Deliver by your power and answer me,
> so that the ones you love may be safe.
> <a name="19:108:7">108:7</a> God has spoken in his sanctuary:
> “I will triumph! I will parcel out Shechem,
> the valley of Succoth I will measure off.
> <a name="19:108:8">108:8</a> Gilead belongs to me,
> as does Manasseh!
> Ephraim is my helmet,
> Judah my royal scepter.
> <a name="19:108:9">108:9</a> Moab is my wash basin.
> I will make Edom serve me.
> I will shout in triumph over Philistia.”
> <a name="19:108:10">108:10</a> Who will lead me into the fortified city?
> Who will bring me to Edom?
> <a name="19:108:11">108:11</a> Have you not rejected us, O God?
> O God, you do not go into battle with our armies.
> <a name="19:108:12">108:12</a> Give us help against the enemy,
> for any help men might offer is futile.
> <a name="19:108:13">108:13</a> By God’s power we will conquer;
> he will trample down our enemies.

### Psalm 109

For the music director, a psalm of David.

> <a name="19:109:1">109:1</a> O God whom I praise, do not ignore me!
> <a name="19:109:2">109:2</a> For they say cruel and deceptive things to me;
> they lie to me.
> <a name="19:109:3">109:3</a> They surround me and say hateful things;
> they attack me for no reason.
> <a name="19:109:4">109:4</a> They repay my love with accusations,
> but I continue to pray.
> <a name="19:109:5">109:5</a> They repay me evil for good,
> and hate for love.
> <a name="19:109:6">109:6</a> Appoint an evil man to testify against him!
> May an accuser stand at his right side!
> <a name="19:109:7">109:7</a> When he is judged, he will be found guilty!
> Then his prayer will be regarded as sinful.
> <a name="19:109:8">109:8</a> May his days be few!
> May another take his job!
> <a name="19:109:9">109:9</a> May his children be fatherless,
> and his wife a widow!
> <a name="19:109:10">109:10</a> May his children roam around begging,
> asking for handouts as they leave their ruined home!
> <a name="19:109:11">109:11</a> May the creditor seize all he owns!
> May strangers loot his property!
> <a name="19:109:12">109:12</a> May no one show him kindness!
> May no one have compassion on his fatherless children!
> <a name="19:109:13">109:13</a> May his descendants be cut off!
> May the memory of them be wiped out by the time the next generation arrives!
> <a name="19:109:14">109:14</a> May his ancestors’ sins be remembered by the Lord!
> May his mother’s sin not be forgotten!
> <a name="19:109:15">109:15</a> May the Lord be constantly aware of them,
> and cut off the memory of his children from the earth!
> <a name="19:109:16">109:16</a> For he never bothered to show kindness;
> he harassed the oppressed and needy,
> and killed the disheartened.
> <a name="19:109:17">109:17</a> He loved to curse others, so those curses have come upon him.
> He had no desire to bless anyone, so he has experienced no blessings.
> <a name="19:109:18">109:18</a> He made cursing a way of life,
> so curses poured into his stomach like water
> and seeped into his bones like oil.
