> <a name="19:109:19">109:19</a> May a curse attach itself to him, like a garment one puts on,
> or a belt one wears continually!
> <a name="19:109:20">109:20</a> May the Lord repay my accusers in this way,
> those who say evil things about me!
> <a name="19:109:21">109:21</a> O sovereign Lord,
> intervene on my behalf for the sake of your reputation!
> Because your loyal love is good, deliver me!
> <a name="19:109:22">109:22</a> For I am oppressed and needy,
> and my heart beats violently within me.
> <a name="19:109:23">109:23</a> I am fading away like a shadow at the end of the day;
> I am shaken off like a locust.
> <a name="19:109:24">109:24</a> I am so starved my knees shake;
> I have turned into skin and bones.
> <a name="19:109:25">109:25</a> I am disdained by them.
> When they see me, they shake their heads.
> <a name="19:109:26">109:26</a> Help me, O Lord my God!
> Because you are faithful to me, deliver me!
> <a name="19:109:27">109:27</a> Then they will realize this is your work,
> and that you, Lord, have accomplished it.
> <a name="19:109:28">109:28</a> They curse, but you will bless.
> When they attack, they will be humiliated,
> but your servant will rejoice.
> <a name="19:109:29">109:29</a> My accusers will be covered with shame,
> and draped in humiliation as if it were a robe.
> <a name="19:109:30">109:30</a> I will thank the Lord profusely,
> in the middle of a crowd I will praise him,
> <a name="19:109:31">109:31</a> because he stands at the right hand of the needy,
> to deliver him from those who threaten his life.

### Psalm 110

A psalm of David.

> <a name="19:110:1">110:1</a> Here is the Lord’s proclamation to my lord:
> “Sit down at my right hand until I make your enemies your footstool!”
> <a name="19:110:2">110:2</a> The Lord extends your dominion from Zion.
> Rule in the midst of your enemies!
> <a name="19:110:3">110:3</a> Your people willingly follow you when you go into battle.
> On the holy hills at sunrise the dew of your youth belongs to you.
> <a name="19:110:4">110:4</a> The Lord makes this promise on oath and will not revoke it:
> “You are an eternal priest after the pattern of Melchizedek.”
> <a name="19:110:5">110:5</a> O sovereign Lord, at your right hand
> he strikes down kings in the day he unleashes his anger.
> <a name="19:110:6">110:6</a> He executes judgment against the nations;
> he fills the valleys with corpses;
> he shatters their heads over the vast battlefield.
> <a name="19:110:7">110:7</a> From the stream along the road he drinks;
> then he lifts up his head.

### Psalm 111

> <a name="19:111:1">111:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> I will give thanks to the Lord with my whole heart,
> in the assembly of the godly and the congregation.
> <a name="19:111:2">111:2</a> The Lord’s deeds are great,
> eagerly awaited by all who desire them.
> <a name="19:111:3">111:3</a> His work is majestic and glorious,
> and his faithfulness endures forever.
> <a name="19:111:4">111:4</a> He does amazing things that will be remembered;
> the Lord is merciful and compassionate.
> <a name="19:111:5">111:5</a> He gives food to his faithful followers;
> he always remembers his covenant.
> <a name="19:111:6">111:6</a> He announced that he would do mighty deeds for his people,
> giving them a land that belonged to other nations.
> <a name="19:111:7">111:7</a> His acts are characterized by faithfulness and justice;
> all his precepts are reliable.
> <a name="19:111:8">111:8</a> They are forever firm,
> and should be faithfully and properly carried out.
> <a name="19:111:9">111:9</a> He delivered his people;
> he ordained that his covenant be observed forever.
> His name is holy and awesome.
> <a name="19:111:10">111:10</a> To obey the Lord is the fundamental principle for wise living;
> all who carry out his precepts acquire good moral insight.
> He will receive praise forever.

### Psalm 112

> <a name="19:112:1">112:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> How happy is the one who obeys the Lord,
> who takes great delight in keeping his commands.
> <a name="19:112:2">112:2</a> His descendants will be powerful on the earth;
> the godly will be blessed.
> <a name="19:112:3">112:3</a> His house contains wealth and riches;
> his integrity endures.
> <a name="19:112:4">112:4</a> In the darkness a light shines for the godly,
> for each one who is merciful, compassionate, and just.
> <a name="19:112:5">112:5</a> It goes well for the one who generously lends money,
> and conducts his business honestly.
> <a name="19:112:6">112:6</a> For he will never be upended;
> others will always remember one who is just.
> <a name="19:112:7">112:7</a> He does not fear bad news.
> He is confident; he trusts in the Lord.
> <a name="19:112:8">112:8</a> His resolve is firm; he will not succumb to fear
> before he looks in triumph on his enemies.
> <a name="19:112:9">112:9</a> He generously gives to the needy;
> his integrity endures.
> He will be vindicated and honored.
> <a name="19:112:10">112:10</a> When the wicked see this, they will worry;
> they will grind their teeth in frustration and melt away;
> the desire of the wicked will perish.

### Psalm 113

> <a name="19:113:1">113:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Praise, you servants of the Lord,
> praise the name of the Lord!
> <a name="19:113:2">113:2</a> May the Lord’s name be praised
> now and forevermore!
> <a name="19:113:3">113:3</a> From east to west
> the Lord’s name is deserving of praise.
> <a name="19:113:4">113:4</a> The Lord is exalted over all the nations;
> his splendor reaches beyond the sky.
> <a name="19:113:5">113:5</a> Who can compare to the Lord our God,
> who sits on a high throne?
> <a name="19:113:6">113:6</a> He bends down to look
> at the sky and the earth.
> <a name="19:113:7">113:7</a> He raises the poor from the dirt,
> and lifts up the needy from the garbage pile,
> <a name="19:113:8">113:8</a> that he might seat him with princes,
> with the princes of his people.
> <a name="19:113:9">113:9</a> He makes the barren woman of the family
> a happy mother of children.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 114

> <a name="19:114:1">114:1</a> When Israel left Egypt,
> when the family of Jacob left a foreign nation behind,
> <a name="19:114:2">114:2</a> Judah became his sanctuary,
> Israel his kingdom.
> <a name="19:114:3">114:3</a> The sea looked and fled;
> the Jordan River turned back.
> <a name="19:114:4">114:4</a> The mountains skipped like rams,
> the hills like lambs.
> <a name="19:114:5">114:5</a> Why do you flee, O sea?
> Why do you turn back, O Jordan River?
> <a name="19:114:6">114:6</a> Why do you skip like rams, O mountains,
> like lambs, O hills?
> <a name="19:114:7">114:7</a> Tremble, O earth, before the sovereign Master—
> before the God of Jacob,
> <a name="19:114:8">114:8</a> who turned a rock into a pool of water,
> a hard rock into springs of water!

### Psalm 115

> <a name="19:115:1">115:1</a> Not to us, O Lord, not to us!
> But to your name bring honor,
> for the sake of your loyal love and faithfulness.
> <a name="19:115:2">115:2</a> Why should the nations say,
> “Where is their God?”
> <a name="19:115:3">115:3</a> Our God is in heaven!
> He does whatever he pleases!
> <a name="19:115:4">115:4</a> Their idols are made of silver and gold—
> they are man-made.
> <a name="19:115:5">115:5</a> They have mouths, but cannot speak,
> eyes, but cannot see,
> <a name="19:115:6">115:6</a> ears, but cannot hear,
> noses, but cannot smell,
> <a name="19:115:7">115:7</a> hands, but cannot touch,
> feet, but cannot walk.
> They cannot even clear their throats.
> <a name="19:115:8">115:8</a> Those who make them will end up like them,
> as will everyone who trusts in them.
> <a name="19:115:9">115:9</a> O Israel, trust in the Lord!
> He is their deliverer and protector.
> <a name="19:115:10">115:10</a> O family of Aaron, trust in the Lord!
> He is their deliverer and protector.
> <a name="19:115:11">115:11</a> You loyal followers of the Lord, trust in the Lord!
> He is their deliverer and protector.
> <a name="19:115:12">115:12</a> The Lord takes notice of us, he will bless—
> he will bless the family of Israel,
> he will bless the family of Aaron.
> <a name="19:115:13">115:13</a> He will bless his loyal followers,
> both young and old.
> <a name="19:115:14">115:14</a> May he increase your numbers,
> yours and your children’s!
> <a name="19:115:15">115:15</a> May you be blessed by the Lord,
> the creator of heaven and earth!
> <a name="19:115:16">115:16</a> The heavens belong to the Lord,
> but the earth he has given to mankind.
> <a name="19:115:17">115:17</a> The dead do not praise the Lord,
> nor do any of those who descend into the silence of death.
> <a name="19:115:18">115:18</a> But we will praise the Lord
> now and forevermore.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 116

> <a name="19:116:1">116:1</a> I love the Lord
> because he heard my plea for mercy,
> <a name="19:116:2">116:2</a> and listened to me.
> As long as I live, I will call to him when I need help.
> <a name="19:116:3">116:3</a> The ropes of death tightened around me,
> the snares of Sheol confronted me.
> I was confronted with trouble and sorrow.
> <a name="19:116:4">116:4</a> I called on the name of the Lord,
> “Please Lord, rescue my life!”
> <a name="19:116:5">116:5</a> The Lord is merciful and fair;
> our God is compassionate.
> <a name="19:116:6">116:6</a> The Lord protects the untrained;
> I was in serious trouble and he delivered me.
> <a name="19:116:7">116:7</a> Rest once more, my soul,
> for the Lord has vindicated you.
> <a name="19:116:8">116:8</a> Yes, Lord, you rescued my life from death,
> and kept my feet from stumbling.
> <a name="19:116:9">116:9</a> I will serve the Lord
> in the land of the living.
> <a name="19:116:10">116:10</a> I had faith when I said,
> “I am severely oppressed.”
> <a name="19:116:11">116:11</a> I rashly declared,
> “All men are liars.”
> <a name="19:116:12">116:12</a> How can I repay the Lord
> for all his acts of kindness to me?
> <a name="19:116:13">116:13</a> I will celebrate my deliverance,
> and call on the name of the Lord.
> <a name="19:116:14">116:14</a> I will fulfill my vows to the Lord
> before all his people.
> <a name="19:116:15">116:15</a> The Lord values
> the lives of his faithful followers.
> <a name="19:116:16">116:16</a> Yes, Lord! I am indeed your servant;
> I am your lowest slave.
> You saved me from death.
> <a name="19:116:17">116:17</a> I will present a thank offering to you,
> and call on the name of the Lord.
> <a name="19:116:18">116:18</a> I will fulfill my vows to the Lord
> before all his people,
> <a name="19:116:19">116:19</a> in the courts of the Lord’s temple,
> in your midst, O Jerusalem.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 117

> <a name="19:117:1">117:1</a> Praise the Lord, all you nations!
> Applaud him, all you foreigners!
> <a name="19:117:2">117:2</a> For his loyal love towers over us,
> and the Lord’s faithfulness endures.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 118

> <a name="19:118:1">118:1</a> Give thanks to the Lord, for he is good
> and his loyal love endures!
> <a name="19:118:2">118:2</a> Let Israel say,
> “Yes, his loyal love endures!”
> <a name="19:118:3">118:3</a> Let the family of Aaron say,
> “Yes, his loyal love endures!”
> <a name="19:118:4">118:4</a> Let the loyal followers of the Lord say,
> “Yes, his loyal love endures!”
> <a name="19:118:5">118:5</a> In my distress I cried out to the Lord.
> The Lord answered me and put me in a wide open place.
> <a name="19:118:6">118:6</a> The Lord is on my side, I am not afraid!
> What can people do to me?
> <a name="19:118:7">118:7</a> The Lord is on my side as my helper.
> I look in triumph on those who hate me.
> <a name="19:118:8">118:8</a> It is better to take shelter in the Lord
> than to trust in people.
> <a name="19:118:9">118:9</a> It is better to take shelter in the Lord
> than to trust in princes.
> <a name="19:118:10">118:10</a> All the nations surrounded me.
> Indeed, in the name of the Lord I pushed them away.
> <a name="19:118:11">118:11</a> They surrounded me, yes, they surrounded me.
> Indeed, in the name of the Lord I pushed them away.
> <a name="19:118:12">118:12</a> They surrounded me like bees.
> But they disappeared as quickly as a fire among thorns.
> Indeed, in the name of the Lord I pushed them away.
> <a name="19:118:13">118:13</a> “You aggressively attacked me and tried to knock me down,
> but the Lord helped me.
> <a name="19:118:14">118:14</a> The Lord gives me strength and protects me;
> he has become my deliverer.”
> <a name="19:118:15">118:15</a> They celebrate deliverance in the tents of the godly.
> The Lord’s right hand conquers,
> <a name="19:118:16">118:16</a> the Lord’s right hand gives victory,
> the Lord’s right hand conquers.
> <a name="19:118:17">118:17</a> I will not die, but live,
> and I will proclaim what the Lord has done.
> <a name="19:118:18">118:18</a> The Lord severely punished me,
> but he did not hand me over to death.
> <a name="19:118:19">118:19</a> Open for me the gates of the just king’s temple!
> I will enter through them and give thanks to the Lord.
> <a name="19:118:20">118:20</a> This is the Lord’s gate—
> the godly enter through it.
> <a name="19:118:21">118:21</a> I will give you thanks, for you answered me,
> and have become my deliverer.
> <a name="19:118:22">118:22</a> The stone which the builders discarded
> has become the cornerstone.
> <a name="19:118:23">118:23</a> This is the Lord’s work.
> We consider it amazing!
> <a name="19:118:24">118:24</a> This is the day the Lord has brought about.
> We will be happy and rejoice in it.
> <a name="19:118:25">118:25</a> Please Lord, deliver!
> Please Lord, grant us success!
> <a name="19:118:26">118:26</a> May the one who comes in the name of the Lord be blessed!
> We will pronounce blessings on you in the Lord’s temple.
> <a name="19:118:27">118:27</a> The Lord is God and he has delivered us.
> Tie the offering with ropes
> to the horns of the altar!
> <a name="19:118:28">118:28</a> You are my God and I will give you thanks!
> You are my God and I will praise you!
> <a name="19:118:29">118:29</a> Give thanks to the Lord, for he is good
> and his loyal love endures!

### Psalm 119

#### א (Alef)

> <a name="19:119:1">119:1</a> How happy are those whose actions are blameless,
> who obey the law of the Lord.
> <a name="19:119:2">119:2</a> How happy are those who observe his rules,
> and seek him with all their heart,
> <a name="19:119:3">119:3</a> who, moreover, do no wrong,
> but obey his demands.
> <a name="19:119:4">119:4</a> You demand that your precepts
> be carefully kept.
> <a name="19:119:5">119:5</a> If only I were predisposed
> to keep your statutes!
> <a name="19:119:6">119:6</a> Then I would not be ashamed,
> if I were focused on all your commands.
> <a name="19:119:7">119:7</a> I will give you sincere thanks,
> when I learn your just regulations.
> <a name="19:119:8">119:8</a> I will keep your statutes.
> Do not completely abandon me!

#### ב (Bet)

> <a name="19:119:9">119:9</a> How can a young person maintain a pure lifestyle?
> By following your instructions!
> <a name="19:119:10">119:10</a> With all my heart I seek you.
> Do not allow me to stray from your commands!
> <a name="19:119:11">119:11</a> In my heart I store up your words,
> so I might not sin against you.
> <a name="19:119:12">119:12</a> You deserve praise, O Lord!
> Teach me your statutes!
> <a name="19:119:13">119:13</a> With my lips I proclaim
> all the regulations you have revealed.
> <a name="19:119:14">119:14</a> I rejoice in the lifestyle prescribed by your rules
> as if they were riches of all kinds.
> <a name="19:119:15">119:15</a> I will meditate on your precepts
> and focus on your demands.
> <a name="19:119:16">119:16</a> I find delight in your statutes;
> I do not forget your instructions.

#### ג (Gimel)

> <a name="19:119:17">119:17</a> Be kind to your servant!
> Then I will live and keep your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:18">119:18</a> Uncover my eyes so I can gaze at
> marvelous things out of your law!
> <a name="19:119:19">119:19</a> I am like a foreigner temporarily residing in a land.
> Do not hide your commands from me!
> <a name="19:119:20">119:20</a> I desperately long to know
> your regulations at all times.
> <a name="19:119:21">119:21</a> You reprimand arrogant people.
> Those who stray from your commands are doomed.
> <a name="19:119:22">119:22</a> Spare me shame and humiliation,
> for I observe your rules.
> <a name="19:119:23">119:23</a> Though rulers plot and slander me,
> your servant meditates on your statutes.
> <a name="19:119:24">119:24</a> Yes, I find delight in your rules;
> they give me guidance.

#### ד (Dalet)

> <a name="19:119:25">119:25</a> I sprawl in the dirt.
> Revive me with your assuring word!
> <a name="19:119:26">119:26</a> I told you about my circumstances and you answered me.
> Teach me your statutes!
> <a name="19:119:27">119:27</a> Help me to understand what your precepts mean!
> Then I can meditate on your amazing teachings.
> <a name="19:119:28">119:28</a> I collapse from grief.
> Sustain me by your assuring word!
> <a name="19:119:29">119:29</a> Remove me from the path of deceit!
> Graciously give me your law!
> <a name="19:119:30">119:30</a> I choose the path of faithfulness;
> I am committed to your regulations.
> <a name="19:119:31">119:31</a> I hold fast to your rules.
> O Lord, do not let me be ashamed!
> <a name="19:119:32">119:32</a> I run along in the path of your commands,
> for you give me the capacity to do so.

#### ה (He)

> <a name="19:119:33">119:33</a> Teach me, O Lord, the lifestyle prescribed by your statutes,
> so that I might observe it continually.
> <a name="19:119:34">119:34</a> Give me understanding so that I might observe your law,
> and keep it with all my heart.
> <a name="19:119:35">119:35</a> Guide me in the path of your commands,
> for I delight in walking in it.
> <a name="19:119:36">119:36</a> Give me a desire for your rules,
> rather than wealth.
> <a name="19:119:37">119:37</a> Turn my eyes away from what is worthless!
> Revive me with your assuring word!
> <a name="19:119:38">119:38</a> Confirm to your servant your promise,
> which you made to the one who honors you.
> <a name="19:119:39">119:39</a> Take away the insults that I dread!
> Indeed, your regulations are good.
> <a name="19:119:40">119:40</a> Look, I long for your precepts.
> Revive me with your deliverance!

#### ו (Vav)

> <a name="19:119:41">119:41</a> May I experience your loyal love, O Lord,
> and your deliverance, as you promised.
> <a name="19:119:42">119:42</a> Then I will have a response for the one who insults me,
> for I trust in your assuring word.
> <a name="19:119:43">119:43</a> Do not deprive me totally of being able to give a truthful testimony,
> for I wait for your justice.
> <a name="19:119:44">119:44</a> Then I will keep your law continually
> and on into the future.
> <a name="19:119:45">119:45</a> I will be secure,
> for I seek your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:46">119:46</a> I will speak about your regulations before kings
> and not be ashamed.
> <a name="19:119:47">119:47</a> I will find delight in your commands,
> which I love.
> <a name="19:119:48">119:48</a> I will lift my hands to your commands,
> which I love,
> and I will meditate on your statutes.

#### ז (Zayin)

> <a name="19:119:49">119:49</a> Remember your assuring word to your servant,
> for you have given me hope.
> <a name="19:119:50">119:50</a> This is what comforts me in my trouble,
> for your promise revives me.
> <a name="19:119:51">119:51</a> Arrogant people do nothing but scoff at me.
> Yet I do not turn aside from your law.
> <a name="19:119:52">119:52</a> I remember your ancient regulations,
> O Lord, and console myself.
> <a name="19:119:53">119:53</a> Rage takes hold of me because of the wicked,
> those who reject your law.
> <a name="19:119:54">119:54</a> I have sung about your statutes
> in the house where I live.
> <a name="19:119:55">119:55</a> I remember your name during the night, O Lord,
> and I will keep your law.
> <a name="19:119:56">119:56</a> This has been my practice,
> for I observe your precepts.

#### ח (Khet)

> <a name="19:119:57">119:57</a> The Lord is my source of security.
> I have determined to follow your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:58">119:58</a> I seek your favor with all my heart.
> Have mercy on me as you promised!
> <a name="19:119:59">119:59</a> I consider my actions
> and follow your rules.
> <a name="19:119:60">119:60</a> I keep your commands
> eagerly and without delay.
> <a name="19:119:61">119:61</a> The ropes of the wicked tighten around me,
> but I do not forget your law.
> <a name="19:119:62">119:62</a> In the middle of the night I arise to thank you
> for your just regulations.
> <a name="19:119:63">119:63</a> I am a friend of all your loyal followers,
> and of those who keep your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:64">119:64</a> O Lord, your loyal love fills the earth.
> Teach me your statutes!

#### ט (Tet)

> <a name="19:119:65">119:65</a> You are good to your servant,
> O Lord, just as you promised.
> <a name="19:119:66">119:66</a> Teach me proper discernment and understanding!
> For I consider your commands to be reliable.
> <a name="19:119:67">119:67</a> I used to suffer because I would stray off,
> but now I keep your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:68">119:68</a> You are good and you do good.
> Teach me your statutes!
> <a name="19:119:69">119:69</a> Arrogant people smear my reputation with lies,
> but I observe your precepts with all my heart.
> <a name="19:119:70">119:70</a> They are calloused,
> but I find delight in your law.
> <a name="19:119:71">119:71</a> It was good for me to suffer,
> so that I might learn your statutes.
> <a name="19:119:72">119:72</a> The law you have revealed is more important to me
> than thousands of gold and silver shekels.

#### י (Yod)

> <a name="19:119:73">119:73</a> Your hands made me and formed me.
> Give me understanding so that I might learn your commands.
> <a name="19:119:74">119:74</a> Your loyal followers will be glad when they see me,
> for I find hope in your assuring word.
> <a name="19:119:75">119:75</a> I know, Lord, that your regulations are just.
> You disciplined me because of your faithful devotion to me.
> <a name="19:119:76">119:76</a> May your loyal love console me,
> as you promised your servant.
> <a name="19:119:77">119:77</a> May I experience your compassion, so I might live!
> For I find delight in your law.
> <a name="19:119:78">119:78</a> May the arrogant be humiliated, for they have slandered me!
> But I meditate on your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:79">119:79</a> May your loyal followers turn to me,
> those who know your rules.
> <a name="19:119:80">119:80</a> May I be fully committed to your statutes,
> so that I might not be ashamed.

#### כ (Kaf)

> <a name="19:119:81">119:81</a> I desperately long for your deliverance.
> I find hope in your assuring word.
> <a name="19:119:82">119:82</a> My eyes grow tired as I wait for your promise to be fulfilled.
> I say, “When will you comfort me?”
> <a name="19:119:83">119:83</a> For I am like a leather container that shrivels up in a smoke-filled room.
> I do not forget your statutes.
> <a name="19:119:84">119:84</a> How long must your servant endure this?
> When will you judge those who chase me?
> <a name="19:119:85">119:85</a> The arrogant dig pits to trap me,
> which violates your law.
> <a name="19:119:86">119:86</a> All your commands are reliable.
> They chase me without reason. Help me!
> <a name="19:119:87">119:87</a> They have almost destroyed me here on the earth,
> but I do not reject your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:88">119:88</a> Revive me with your loyal love,
> that I might keep the rules you have revealed.

#### ל (Lamed)

> <a name="19:119:89">119:89</a> O Lord, your instructions endure;
> they stand secure in heaven.
> <a name="19:119:90">119:90</a> You demonstrate your faithfulness to all generations.
> You established the earth and it stood firm.
> <a name="19:119:91">119:91</a> Today they stand firm by your decrees,
> for all things are your servants.
> <a name="19:119:92">119:92</a> If I had not found encouragement in your law,
> I would have died in my sorrow.
> <a name="19:119:93">119:93</a> I will never forget your precepts,
> for by them you have revived me.
> <a name="19:119:94">119:94</a> I belong to you. Deliver me!
> For I seek your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:95">119:95</a> The wicked prepare to kill me,
> yet I think about your rules.
> <a name="19:119:96">119:96</a> I realize that everything has its limits,
> but your commands are beyond full comprehension.

#### מ (Mem)

> <a name="19:119:97">119:97</a> O how I love your law!
> All day long I meditate on it.
> <a name="19:119:98">119:98</a> Your law makes me wiser than my enemies,
> for I am always aware of it.
> <a name="19:119:99">119:99</a> I even have more insight than all my teachers,
> for I meditate on your rules.
> <a name="19:119:100">119:100</a> I am more discerning than the older men,
> for I observe your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:101">119:101</a> I stay away from the evil path,
> so that I might keep your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:102">119:102</a> I do not turn aside from your regulations,
> for you teach me.
> <a name="19:119:103">119:103</a> Your words are tastier
> in my mouth than honey!
> <a name="19:119:104">119:104</a> Your precepts give me discernment.
> Therefore I hate all deceitful actions.

#### נ (Nun)

> <a name="19:119:105">119:105</a> Your instructions are a lamp that shows me where to walk,
> and a light that shines on my path.
> <a name="19:119:106">119:106</a> I have vowed and solemnly sworn
> to keep your just regulations.
> <a name="19:119:107">119:107</a> I am suffering a great deal.
> O Lord, revive me with your assuring word!
> <a name="19:119:108">119:108</a> O Lord, please accept the freewill offerings from my mouth!
> Teach me your regulations!
> <a name="19:119:109">119:109</a> My life is in continual danger,
> but I do not forget your law.
> <a name="19:119:110">119:110</a> The wicked lay a snare for me,
> but I do not wander from your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:111">119:111</a> I claim your rules as my permanent possession,
> for they give me joy.
> <a name="19:119:112">119:112</a> I am determined to obey your statutes
> at all times to the very end.

#### ס (Samek)

> <a name="19:119:113">119:113</a> I hate people with divided loyalties,
> but I love your law.
> <a name="19:119:114">119:114</a> You are my hiding place and my shield.
> I find hope in your assuring word.
> <a name="19:119:115">119:115</a> Turn back from me, you evil men,
> so that I might observe the commands of my God.
> <a name="19:119:116">119:116</a> Sustain me as you promised, so that I might live.
> Do not disappoint me!
> <a name="19:119:117">119:117</a> Support me, so that I might be delivered.
> Then I will focus on your statutes continually.
> <a name="19:119:118">119:118</a> You despise all who stray from your statutes,
> for they are deceptive and unreliable.
> <a name="19:119:119">119:119</a> You remove all the wicked of the earth like slag.
> Therefore I love your rules.
> <a name="19:119:120">119:120</a> My body trembles because of my fear of you;
> I am afraid of your judgments.

#### ע (Ayin)

> <a name="19:119:121">119:121</a> I do what is fair and right.
> Do not abandon me to my oppressors!
> <a name="19:119:122">119:122</a> Guarantee the well-being of your servant!
> Do not let the arrogant oppress me!
> <a name="19:119:123">119:123</a> My eyes grow tired as I wait for your deliverance,
> for your reliable promise to be fulfilled.
> <a name="19:119:124">119:124</a> Show your servant your loyal love!
> Teach me your statutes!
> <a name="19:119:125">119:125</a> I am your servant. Give me insight,
> that I might understand your rules.
> <a name="19:119:126">119:126</a> It is time for the Lord to act—
> they break your law!
> <a name="19:119:127">119:127</a> For this reason I love your commands
> more than gold, even pure gold.
> <a name="19:119:128">119:128</a> For this reason I carefully follow all your precepts.
> I hate all deceitful actions.

#### פ (Pe)

> <a name="19:119:129">119:129</a> Your rules are marvelous.
> Therefore I observe them.
> <a name="19:119:130">119:130</a> Your instructions are like a doorway through which the light shines.
> They give insight to the untrained.
> <a name="19:119:131">119:131</a> I open my mouth and gasp,
> because I long for your commands.
> <a name="19:119:132">119:132</a> Turn toward me and extend mercy to me,
> as you typically do to your loyal followers.
> <a name="19:119:133">119:133</a> Direct my steps by your word!
> Do not let any sin dominate me!
> <a name="19:119:134">119:134</a> Deliver me from oppressive men,
> that I might keep your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:135">119:135</a> Smile on your servant!
> Teach me your statutes!
> <a name="19:119:136">119:136</a> Tears stream down from my eyes,
> because they do not keep your law.

#### צ (Tsade)

> <a name="19:119:137">119:137</a> You are just, O Lord,
> and your regulations are fair.
> <a name="19:119:138">119:138</a> The rules you impose are just,
> and absolutely reliable.
> <a name="19:119:139">119:139</a> My devotion consumes me,
> for my enemies forget your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:140">119:140</a> Your word is absolutely pure,
> and your servant loves it.
> <a name="19:119:141">119:141</a> I am insignificant and despised,
> yet I do not forget your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:142">119:142</a> Your justice endures,
> and your law is reliable.
> <a name="19:119:143">119:143</a> Distress and hardship confront me,
> yet I find delight in your commands.
> <a name="19:119:144">119:144</a> Your rules remain just.
> Give me insight that I might live.

#### ק (Qof)

> <a name="19:119:145">119:145</a> I cried out with all my heart, “Answer me, O Lord!
> I will observe your statutes.”
> <a name="19:119:146">119:146</a> I cried out to you, “Deliver me,
> that I might keep your rules.”
> <a name="19:119:147">119:147</a> I am up before dawn crying out.
> I find hope in your assuring word.
> <a name="19:119:148">119:148</a> My eyes anticipate the nighttime hours,
> that I may meditate on your word.
> <a name="19:119:149">119:149</a> Listen to me because of your loyal love!
> O Lord, revive me, as you typically do!
> <a name="19:119:150">119:150</a> Those who are eager to do wrong approach;
> they are far from your law.
> <a name="19:119:151">119:151</a> You are near, O Lord,
> and all your commands are reliable.
> <a name="19:119:152">119:152</a> Long ago I realized that
> you ordained your rules to last.

#### ר (Resh)

> <a name="19:119:153">119:153</a> See my pain and rescue me!
> For I do not forget your law.
> <a name="19:119:154">119:154</a> Fight for me and defend me!
> Revive me with your assuring word!
> <a name="19:119:155">119:155</a> The wicked have no chance for deliverance,
> for they do not seek your statutes.
> <a name="19:119:156">119:156</a> Your compassion is great, O Lord.
> Revive me, as you typically do!
> <a name="19:119:157">119:157</a> The enemies who chase me are numerous.
> Yet I do not turn aside from your rules.
> <a name="19:119:158">119:158</a> I take note of the treacherous and despise them,
> because they do not keep your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:159">119:159</a> See how I love your precepts!
> O Lord, revive me with your loyal love!
> <a name="19:119:160">119:160</a> Your instructions are totally reliable;
> all your just regulations endure.

#### ש (Sin/Shin)

> <a name="19:119:161">119:161</a> Rulers chase me for no reason,
> yet I fear disobeying your instructions.
> <a name="19:119:162">119:162</a> My heart rejoices in your instructions,
> like one who gathers up a great deal of plunder.
> <a name="19:119:163">119:163</a> I hate and despise deceit;
> I love your law.
> <a name="19:119:164">119:164</a> Seven times a day I praise you
> because of your just regulations.
> <a name="19:119:165">119:165</a> Those who love your law are completely secure;
> they are not upended.
> <a name="19:119:166">119:166</a> I hope for your deliverance, O Lord,
> and I obey your commands.
> <a name="19:119:167">119:167</a> I keep your rules;
> I love them greatly.
> <a name="19:119:168">119:168</a> I keep your precepts and rules,
> for you are aware of all my actions.

#### ת (Tav)

> <a name="19:119:169">119:169</a> Listen to my cry for help, O Lord!
> Give me insight by your instructions!
> <a name="19:119:170">119:170</a> Listen to my appeal for mercy!
> Deliver me, as you promised.
> <a name="19:119:171">119:171</a> May praise gush from my lips,
> for you teach me your statutes.
> <a name="19:119:172">119:172</a> May my tongue sing about your instructions,
> for all your commands are just.
> <a name="19:119:173">119:173</a> May your hand help me,
> for I choose to obey your precepts.
> <a name="19:119:174">119:174</a> I long for your deliverance, O Lord;
> I find delight in your law.
> <a name="19:119:175">119:175</a> May I live and praise you!
> May your regulations help me!
> <a name="19:119:176">119:176</a> I am as vulnerable as a straying and lost sheep.
> Come looking for your servant,
> for I do not forget your commands.

### Psalm 120

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:120:1">120:1</a> In my distress I cried out
> to the Lord and he answered me.
> <a name="19:120:2">120:2</a> I said, “O Lord, rescue me
> from those who lie with their lips
> and those who deceive with their tongue.
> <a name="19:120:3">120:3</a> How will he severely punish you,
> you deceptive talker?
> <a name="19:120:4">120:4</a> Here’s how! With the sharp arrows of warriors,
> with arrowheads forged over the hot coals.
> <a name="19:120:5">120:5</a> How miserable I am!
> For I have lived temporarily in Meshech;
> I have resided among the tents of Kedar.
> <a name="19:120:6">120:6</a> For too long I have had to reside
> with those who hate peace.
> <a name="19:120:7">120:7</a> I am committed to peace,
> but when I speak, they want to make war.

### Psalm 121

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:121:1">121:1</a> I look up toward the hills.
> From where does my help come?
> <a name="19:121:2">121:2</a> My help comes from the Lord,
> the Creator of heaven and earth!
> <a name="19:121:3">121:3</a> May he not allow your foot to slip!
> May your protector not sleep!
> <a name="19:121:4">121:4</a> Look! Israel’s protector
> does not sleep or slumber!
> <a name="19:121:5">121:5</a> The Lord is your protector;
> the Lord is the shade at your right hand.
> <a name="19:121:6">121:6</a> The sun will not harm you by day,
> or the moon by night.
> <a name="19:121:7">121:7</a> The Lord will protect you from all harm;
> he will protect your life.
> <a name="19:121:8">121:8</a> The Lord will protect you in all you do,
> now and forevermore.

### Psalm 122

A song of ascents, by David.

> <a name="19:122:1">122:1</a> I was glad because they said to me,
> “We will go to the Lord’s temple.”
> <a name="19:122:2">122:2</a> Our feet are standing
> inside your gates, O Jerusalem.
> <a name="19:122:3">122:3</a> Jerusalem is a city designed
> to accommodate an assembly.
> <a name="19:122:4">122:4</a> The tribes go up there,
> the tribes of the Lord,
> where it is required that Israel
> give thanks to the name of the Lord.
> <a name="19:122:5">122:5</a> Indeed, the leaders sit there on thrones and make legal decisions,
> on the thrones of the house of David.
> <a name="19:122:6">122:6</a> Pray for the peace of Jerusalem!
> May those who love her prosper!
> <a name="19:122:7">122:7</a> May there be peace inside your defenses,
> and prosperity inside your fortresses!
> <a name="19:122:8">122:8</a> For the sake of my brothers and my neighbors
> I will say, “May there be peace in you!”
> <a name="19:122:9">122:9</a> For the sake of the temple of the Lord our God
> I will pray for you to prosper.

### Psalm 123

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:123:1">123:1</a> I look up toward you,
> the one enthroned in heaven.
> <a name="19:123:2">123:2</a> Look, as the eyes of servants look to the hand of their master,
> as the eyes of a female servant look to the hand of her mistress,
> so my eyes will look to the Lord, our God, until he shows us favor.
> <a name="19:123:3">123:3</a> Show us favor, O Lord, show us favor!
> For we have had our fill of humiliation, and then some.
> <a name="19:123:4">123:4</a> We have had our fill
> of the taunts of the self-assured,
> of the contempt of the proud.

### Psalm 124

A song of ascents, by David.

> <a name="19:124:1">124:1</a> “If the Lord had not been on our side”—
> let Israel say this!—
> <a name="19:124:2">124:2</a> if the Lord had not been on our side,
> when men attacked us,
> <a name="19:124:3">124:3</a> they would have swallowed us alive,
> when their anger raged against us.
> <a name="19:124:4">124:4</a> The water would have overpowered us;
> the current would have overwhelmed us.
> <a name="19:124:5">124:5</a> The raging water
> would have overwhelmed us.
> <a name="19:124:6">124:6</a> The Lord deserves praise,
> for he did not hand us over as prey to their teeth.
> <a name="19:124:7">124:7</a> We escaped with our lives, like a bird from a hunter’s snare.
> The snare broke, and we escaped.
> <a name="19:124:8">124:8</a> Our deliverer is the Lord,
> the Creator of heaven and earth.

### Psalm 125

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:125:1">125:1</a> Those who trust in the Lord are like Mount Zion;
> it cannot be upended and will endure forever.
> <a name="19:125:2">125:2</a> As the mountains surround Jerusalem,
> so the Lord surrounds his people,
> now and forevermore.
> <a name="19:125:3">125:3</a> Indeed, the scepter of a wicked king will not settle
> upon the allotted land of the godly.
> Otherwise the godly might
> do what is wrong.
> <a name="19:125:4">125:4</a> Do good, O Lord, to those who are good,
> to the morally upright!
> <a name="19:125:5">125:5</a> As for those who are bent on traveling a sinful path,
> may the Lord remove them, along with those who behave wickedly!
> May Israel experience peace!

### Psalm 126

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:126:1">126:1</a> When the Lord restored the well-being of Zion,
> we thought we were dreaming.
> <a name="19:126:2">126:2</a> At that time we laughed loudly
> and shouted for joy.
> At that time the nations said,
> “The Lord has accomplished great things for these people.”
> <a name="19:126:3">126:3</a> The Lord did indeed accomplish great things for us.
> We were happy.
> <a name="19:126:4">126:4</a> O Lord, restore our well-being,
> just as the streams in the arid south are replenished.
> <a name="19:126:5">126:5</a> Those who shed tears as they plant
> will shout for joy when they reap the harvest.
> <a name="19:126:6">126:6</a> The one who weeps as he walks along, carrying his bag of seed,
> will certainly come in with a shout of joy, carrying his sheaves of grain.

### Psalm 127

A song of ascents, by Solomon.

> <a name="19:127:1">127:1</a> If the Lord does not build a house,
> then those who build it work in vain.
> If the Lord does not guard a city,
> then the watchman stands guard in vain.
> <a name="19:127:2">127:2</a> It is vain for you to rise early, come home late,
> and work so hard for your food.
> Yes, he can provide for those whom he loves even when they sleep.
> <a name="19:127:3">127:3</a> Yes, sons are a gift from the Lord,
> the fruit of the womb is a reward.
> <a name="19:127:4">127:4</a> Sons born during one’s youth
> are like arrows in a warrior’s hand.
> <a name="19:127:5">127:5</a> How happy is the man who fills his quiver with them!
> They will not be put to shame when they confront enemies at the city gate.

### Psalm 128

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:128:1">128:1</a> How happy is every one of the Lord’s loyal followers,
> each one who keeps his commands!
> <a name="19:128:2">128:2</a> You will eat what you worked so hard to grow.
> You will be happy and secure.
> <a name="19:128:3">128:3</a> Your wife will be like a fruitful vine
> in the inner rooms of your house;
> your children will be like olive branches,
> as they sit all around your table.
> <a name="19:128:4">128:4</a> Yes indeed, the man who fears the Lord
> will be blessed in this way.
> <a name="19:128:5">128:5</a> May the Lord bless you from Zion,
> that you might see Jerusalem prosper
> all the days of your life,
> <a name="19:128:6">128:6</a> and that you might see your grandchildren.
> May Israel experience peace!

### Psalm 129

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:129:1">129:1</a> “Since my youth they have often attacked me,”
> let Israel say.
> <a name="19:129:2">129:2</a> “Since my youth they have often attacked me,
> but they have not defeated me.
> <a name="19:129:3">129:3</a> The plowers plowed my back;
> they made their furrows long.
> <a name="19:129:4">129:4</a> The Lord is just;
> he cut the ropes of the wicked.”
> <a name="19:129:5">129:5</a> May all who hate Zion
> be humiliated and turned back!
> <a name="19:129:6">129:6</a> May they be like the grass on the rooftops
> which withers before one can even pull it up,
> <a name="19:129:7">129:7</a> which cannot fill the reaper’s hand,
> or the lap of the one who gathers the grain!
> <a name="19:129:8">129:8</a> Those who pass by will not say,
> “May you experience the Lord’s blessing!
> We pronounce a blessing on you in the name of the Lord.”

### Psalm 130

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:130:1">130:1</a> From the deep water I cry out to you, O Lord.
> <a name="19:130:2">130:2</a> O sovereign Master, listen to me!
> Pay attention to my plea for mercy!
> <a name="19:130:3">130:3</a> If you, O Lord, were to keep track of sins,
> O sovereign Master, who could stand before you?
> <a name="19:130:4">130:4</a> But you are willing to forgive,
> so that you might be honored.
> <a name="19:130:5">130:5</a> I rely on the Lord,
> I rely on him with my whole being;
> I wait for his assuring word.
> <a name="19:130:6">130:6</a> I yearn for the sovereign Master,
> more than watchmen do for the morning,
> yes, more than watchmen do for the morning.
> <a name="19:130:7">130:7</a> O Israel, hope in the Lord,
> for the Lord exhibits loyal love,
> and is more than willing to deliver.
> <a name="19:130:8">130:8</a> He will deliver Israel
> from all the consequences of their sins.

### Psalm 131

A song of ascents, by David.

> <a name="19:131:1">131:1</a> O Lord, my heart is not proud,
> nor do I have a haughty look.
> I do not have great aspirations,
> or concern myself with things that are beyond me.
> <a name="19:131:2">131:2</a> Indeed I am composed and quiet,
> like a young child carried by its mother;
> I am content like the young child I carry.
> <a name="19:131:3">131:3</a> O Israel, hope in the Lord
> now and forevermore!

### Psalm 132

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:132:1">132:1</a> O Lord, for David’s sake remember
> all his strenuous effort,
> <a name="19:132:2">132:2</a> and how he made a vow to the Lord,
> and swore an oath to the powerful ruler of Jacob.
> <a name="19:132:3">132:3</a> He said, “I will not enter my own home,
> or get into my bed.
> <a name="19:132:4">132:4</a> I will not allow my eyes to sleep,
> or my eyelids to slumber,
> <a name="19:132:5">132:5</a> until I find a place for the Lord,
> a fine dwelling place for the powerful ruler of Jacob.”
> <a name="19:132:6">132:6</a> Look, we heard about it in Ephrathah,
> we found it in the territory of Jaar.
> <a name="19:132:7">132:7</a> Let us go to his dwelling place!
> Let us worship before his footstool!
> <a name="19:132:8">132:8</a> Ascend, O Lord, to your resting place,
> you and the ark of your strength!
> <a name="19:132:9">132:9</a> May your priests be clothed with integrity!
> May your loyal followers shout for joy!
> <a name="19:132:10">132:10</a> For the sake of David, your servant,
> do not reject your chosen king!
> <a name="19:132:11">132:11</a> The Lord made a reliable promise to David;
> he will not go back on his word.
> He said, “I will place one of your descendants on your throne.
> <a name="19:132:12">132:12</a> If your sons keep my covenant
> and the rules I teach them,
> their sons will also sit on your throne forever.”
> <a name="19:132:13">132:13</a> Certainly the Lord has chosen Zion;
> he decided to make it his home.
> <a name="19:132:14">132:14</a> He said, “This will be my resting place forever;
> I will live here, for I have chosen it.
> <a name="19:132:15">132:15</a> I will abundantly supply what she needs;
> I will give her poor all the food they need.
> <a name="19:132:16">132:16</a> I will protect her priests,
> and her godly people will shout exuberantly.
> <a name="19:132:17">132:17</a> There I will make David strong;
> I have determined that my chosen king’s dynasty will continue.
> <a name="19:132:18">132:18</a> I will humiliate his enemies,
> and his crown will shine.

### Psalm 133

A song of ascents, by David.

> <a name="19:133:1">133:1</a> Look! How good and how pleasant it is
> when brothers live together!
> <a name="19:133:2">133:2</a> It is like fine oil poured on the head
> which flows down the beard—
> Aaron’s beard,
> and then flows down his garments.
> <a name="19:133:3">133:3</a> It is like the dew of Hermon,
> which flows down upon the hills of Zion.
> Indeed that is where the Lord has decreed
> a blessing will be available—eternal life.

### Psalm 134

A song of ascents.

> <a name="19:134:1">134:1</a> Attention! Praise the Lord,
> all you servants of the Lord,
> who serve in the Lord’s temple during the night.
> <a name="19:134:2">134:2</a> Lift your hands toward the sanctuary
> and praise the Lord!
> <a name="19:134:3">134:3</a> May the Lord, the Creator of heaven and earth,
> bless you from Zion!

### Psalm 135

> <a name="19:135:1">135:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Praise the name of the Lord!
> Offer praise, you servants of the Lord,
> <a name="19:135:2">135:2</a> who serve in the Lord’s temple,
> in the courts of the temple of our God.
> <a name="19:135:3">135:3</a> Praise the Lord, for the Lord is good!
> Sing praises to his name, for it is pleasant!
> <a name="19:135:4">135:4</a> Indeed, the Lord has chosen Jacob for himself,
> Israel to be his special possession.
> <a name="19:135:5">135:5</a> Yes, I know the Lord is great,
> and our sovereign Master is superior to all gods.
> <a name="19:135:6">135:6</a> He does whatever he pleases
> in heaven and on earth,
> in the seas and all the ocean depths.
> <a name="19:135:7">135:7</a> He causes the clouds to arise from the end of the earth,
> makes lightning bolts accompany the rain,
> and brings the wind out of his storehouses.
> <a name="19:135:8">135:8</a> He struck down the firstborn of Egypt,
> including both men and animals.
> <a name="19:135:9">135:9</a> He performed awesome deeds and acts of judgment
> in your midst, O Egypt,
> against Pharaoh and all his servants.
> <a name="19:135:10">135:10</a> He defeated many nations,
> and killed mighty kings—
> <a name="19:135:11">135:11</a> Sihon, king of the Amorites,
> and Og, king of Bashan,
> and all the kingdoms of Canaan.
> <a name="19:135:12">135:12</a> He gave their land as an inheritance,
> as an inheritance to Israel his people.
> <a name="19:135:13">135:13</a> O Lord, your name endures,
> your reputation, O Lord, lasts.
> <a name="19:135:14">135:14</a> For the Lord vindicates his people,
> and has compassion on his servants.
> <a name="19:135:15">135:15</a> The nations’ idols are made of silver and gold,
> they are man-made.
> <a name="19:135:16">135:16</a> They have mouths, but cannot speak,
> eyes, but cannot see,
> <a name="19:135:17">135:17</a> and ears, but cannot hear.
> Indeed, they cannot breathe.
> <a name="19:135:18">135:18</a> Those who make them will end up like them,
> as will everyone who trusts in them.
> <a name="19:135:19">135:19</a> O family of Israel, praise the Lord!
> O family of Aaron, praise the Lord!
> <a name="19:135:20">135:20</a> O family of Levi, praise the Lord!
> You loyal followers of the Lord, praise the Lord!
> <a name="19:135:21">135:21</a> The Lord deserves praise in Zion—
> he who dwells in Jerusalem.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 136

> <a name="19:136:1">136:1</a> Give thanks to the Lord, for he is good,
> for his loyal love endures.
> <a name="19:136:2">136:2</a> Give thanks to the God of gods,
> for his loyal love endures.
> <a name="19:136:3">136:3</a> Give thanks to the Lord of lords,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:4">136:4</a> to the one who performs magnificent, amazing deeds all by himself,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:5">136:5</a> to the one who used wisdom to make the heavens,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:6">136:6</a> to the one who spread out the earth over the water,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:7">136:7</a> to the one who made the great lights,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:8">136:8</a> the sun to rule by day,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:9">136:9</a> the moon and stars to rule by night,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:10">136:10</a> to the one who struck down the firstborn of Egypt,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:11">136:11</a> and led Israel out from their midst,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:12">136:12</a> with a strong hand and an outstretched arm,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:13">136:13</a> to the one who divided the Red Sea in two,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:14">136:14</a> and led Israel through its midst,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:15">136:15</a> and tossed Pharaoh and his army into the Red Sea,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:16">136:16</a> to the one who led his people through the wilderness,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:17">136:17</a> to the one who struck down great kings,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:18">136:18</a> and killed powerful kings,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:19">136:19</a> Sihon, king of the Amorites,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:20">136:20</a> Og, king of Bashan,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:21">136:21</a> and gave their land as an inheritance,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:22">136:22</a> as an inheritance to Israel his servant,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:23">136:23</a> to the one who remembered us when we were down,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:24">136:24</a> and snatched us away from our enemies,
> for his loyal love endures,
> <a name="19:136:25">136:25</a> to the one who gives food to all living things,
> for his loyal love endures.
> <a name="19:136:26">136:26</a> Give thanks to the God of heaven,
> for his loyal love endures!

### Psalm 137

> <a name="19:137:1">137:1</a> By the rivers of Babylon
> we sit down and weep
> when we remember Zion.
> <a name="19:137:2">137:2</a> On the poplars in her midst
> we hang our harps,
> <a name="19:137:3">137:3</a> for there our captors ask us to compose songs;
> those who mock us demand that we be happy, saying:
> “Sing for us a song about Zion!”
> <a name="19:137:4">137:4</a> How can we sing a song to the Lord
> in a foreign land?
> <a name="19:137:5">137:5</a> If I forget you, O Jerusalem,
> may my right hand be crippled!
> <a name="19:137:6">137:6</a> May my tongue stick to the roof of my mouth,
> if I do not remember you,
> and do not give Jerusalem priority
> over whatever gives me the most joy.
> <a name="19:137:7">137:7</a> Remember, O Lord, what the Edomites did
> on the day Jerusalem fell.
> They said, “Tear it down, tear it down,
> right to its very foundation!”
> <a name="19:137:8">137:8</a> O daughter Babylon, soon to be devastated!
> How happy will be the one who repays you
> for what you dished out to us!
> <a name="19:137:9">137:9</a> How happy will be the one who grabs your babies
> and smashes them on a rock!

### Psalm 138

By David.

> <a name="19:138:1">138:1</a> I will give you thanks with all my heart;
> before the heavenly assembly I will sing praises to you.
> <a name="19:138:2">138:2</a> I will bow down toward your holy temple,
> and give thanks to your name,
> because of your loyal love and faithfulness,
> for you have exalted your promise above the entire sky.
> <a name="19:138:3">138:3</a> When I cried out for help, you answered me.
> You made me bold and energized me.
> <a name="19:138:4">138:4</a> Let all the kings of the earth give thanks to you, O Lord,
> when they hear the words you speak.
> <a name="19:138:5">138:5</a> Let them sing about the Lord’s deeds,
> for the Lord’s splendor is magnificent.
> <a name="19:138:6">138:6</a> Though the Lord is exalted, he takes note of the lowly,
> and recognizes the proud from far away.
> <a name="19:138:7">138:7</a> Even when I must walk in the midst of danger, you revive me.
> You oppose my angry enemies,
> and your right hand delivers me.
> <a name="19:138:8">138:8</a> The Lord avenges me.
> O Lord, your loyal love endures.
> Do not abandon those whom you have made!

### Psalm 139

For the music director, a psalm of David.

> <a name="19:139:1">139:1</a> O Lord, you examine me and know.
> <a name="19:139:2">139:2</a> You know when I sit down and when I get up;
> even from far away you understand my motives.
> <a name="19:139:3">139:3</a> You carefully observe me when I travel or when I lie down to rest;
> you are aware of everything I do.
> <a name="19:139:4">139:4</a> Certainly my tongue does not frame a word
> without you, O Lord, being thoroughly aware of it.
> <a name="19:139:5">139:5</a> You squeeze me in from behind and in front;
> you place your hand on me.
> <a name="19:139:6">139:6</a> Your knowledge is beyond my comprehension;
> it is so far beyond me, I am unable to fathom it.
> <a name="19:139:7">139:7</a> Where can I go to escape your spirit?
> Where can I flee to escape your presence?
> <a name="19:139:8">139:8</a> If I were to ascend to heaven, you would be there.
> If I were to sprawl out in Sheol, there you would be.
> <a name="19:139:9">139:9</a> If I were to fly away on the wings of the dawn,
> and settle down on the other side of the sea,
> <a name="19:139:10">139:10</a> even there your hand would guide me,
> your right hand would grab hold of me.
> <a name="19:139:11">139:11</a> If I were to say, “Certainly the darkness will cover me,
> and the light will turn to night all around me,”
> <a name="19:139:12">139:12</a> even the darkness is not too dark for you to see,
> and the night is as bright as day;
> darkness and light are the same to you.
> <a name="19:139:13">139:13</a> Certainly you made my mind and heart;
> you wove me together in my mother’s womb.
> <a name="19:139:14">139:14</a> I will give you thanks because your deeds are awesome and amazing.
> You knew me thoroughly;
> <a name="19:139:15">139:15</a> my bones were not hidden from you,
> when I was made in secret
> and sewed together in the depths of the earth.
> <a name="19:139:16">139:16</a> Your eyes saw me when I was inside the womb.
> All the days ordained for me
> were recorded in your scroll
> before one of them came into existence.
> <a name="19:139:17">139:17</a> How difficult it is for me to fathom your thoughts about me, O God!
> How vast are their sum total!
> <a name="19:139:18">139:18</a> If I tried to count them,
> they would outnumber the grains of sand.
> Even if I finished counting them,
> I would still have to contend with you.
> <a name="19:139:19">139:19</a> If only you would kill the wicked, O God!
> Get away from me, you violent men!
> <a name="19:139:20">139:20</a> They rebel against you and act deceitfully;
> your enemies lie.
> <a name="19:139:21">139:21</a> O Lord, do I not hate those who hate you,
> and despise those who oppose you?
> <a name="19:139:22">139:22</a> I absolutely hate them,
> they have become my enemies!
> <a name="19:139:23">139:23</a> Examine me, and probe my thoughts!
> Test me, and know my concerns!
> <a name="19:139:24">139:24</a> See if there is any idolatrous tendency in me,
> and lead me in the reliable ancient path!

### Psalm 140

For the music director; a psalm of David.

> <a name="19:140:1">140:1</a> O Lord, rescue me from wicked men!
> Protect me from violent men,
> <a name="19:140:2">140:2</a> who plan ways to harm me.
> All day long they stir up conflict.
> <a name="19:140:3">140:3</a> Their tongues wound like a serpent;
> a viper’s venom is behind their lips. (Selah)
> <a name="19:140:4">140:4</a> O Lord, shelter me from the power of the wicked!
> Protect me from violent men,
> who plan to knock me over.
> <a name="19:140:5">140:5</a> Proud men hide a snare for me;
> evil men spread a net by the path;
> they set traps for me. (Selah)
> <a name="19:140:6">140:6</a> I say to the Lord, “You are my God.”
> O Lord, pay attention to my plea for mercy!
> <a name="19:140:7">140:7</a> O sovereign Lord, my strong deliverer,
> you shield my head in the day of battle.
> <a name="19:140:8">140:8</a> O Lord, do not let the wicked have their way!
> Do not allow their plan to succeed when they attack! (Selah)
> <a name="19:140:9">140:9</a> As for the heads of those who surround me—
> may the harm done by their lips overwhelm them!
> <a name="19:140:10">140:10</a> May he rain down fiery coals upon them!
> May he throw them into the fire!
> From bottomless pits they will not escape.
> <a name="19:140:11">140:11</a> A slanderer will not endure on the earth;
> calamity will hunt down a violent man and strike him down.
> <a name="19:140:12">140:12</a> I know that the Lord defends the cause of the oppressed
> and vindicates the poor.
> <a name="19:140:13">140:13</a> Certainly the godly will give thanks to your name;
> the morally upright will live in your presence.

### Psalm 141

A psalm of David.

> <a name="19:141:1">141:1</a> O Lord, I cry out to you. Come quickly to me!
> Pay attention to me when I cry out to you!
> <a name="19:141:2">141:2</a> May you accept my prayer like incense,
> my uplifted hands like the evening offering!
> <a name="19:141:3">141:3</a> O Lord, place a guard on my mouth!
> Protect the opening of my lips!
> <a name="19:141:4">141:4</a> Do not let me have evil desires,
> or participate in sinful activities
> with men who behave wickedly.
> I will not eat their delicacies.
> <a name="19:141:5">141:5</a> May the godly strike me in love and correct me!
> May my head not refuse choice oil!
> Indeed, my prayer is a witness against their evil deeds.
> <a name="19:141:6">141:6</a> They will be thrown down the side of a cliff by their judges.
> They will listen to my words, for they are pleasant.
> <a name="19:141:7">141:7</a> As when one plows and breaks up the soil,
> so our bones are scattered at the mouth of Sheol.
> <a name="19:141:8">141:8</a> Surely I am looking to you, O sovereign Lord.
> In you I take shelter.
> Do not expose me to danger!
> <a name="19:141:9">141:9</a> Protect me from the snare they have laid for me,
> and the traps the evildoers have set.
> <a name="19:141:10">141:10</a> Let the wicked fall into their own nets,
> while I escape.

### Psalm 142

A well-written song by David, when he was in the cave; a prayer.

> <a name="19:142:1">142:1</a> To the Lord I cry out;
> to the Lord I plead for mercy.
> <a name="19:142:2">142:2</a> I pour out my lament before him;
> I tell him about my troubles.
> <a name="19:142:3">142:3</a> Even when my strength leaves me,
> you watch my footsteps.
> In the path where I walk
> they have hidden a snare for me.
> <a name="19:142:4">142:4</a> Look to the right and see!
> No one cares about me.
> I have nowhere to run;
> no one is concerned about my life.
> <a name="19:142:5">142:5</a> I cry out to you, O Lord;
> I say, “You are my shelter,
> my security in the land of the living.”
> <a name="19:142:6">142:6</a> Listen to my cry for help,
> for I am in serious trouble!
> Rescue me from those who chase me,
> for they are stronger than I am.
> <a name="19:142:7">142:7</a> Free me from prison,
> that I may give thanks to your name.
> Because of me the godly will assemble,
> for you will vindicate me.

### Psalm 143

A psalm of David.

> <a name="19:143:1">143:1</a> O Lord, hear my prayer!
> Pay attention to my plea for help!
> Because of your faithfulness and justice, answer me!
> <a name="19:143:2">143:2</a> Do not sit in judgment on your servant,
> for no one alive is innocent before you.
> <a name="19:143:3">143:3</a> Certainly my enemies chase me.
> They smash me into the ground.
> They force me to live in dark regions,
> like those who have been dead for ages.
> <a name="19:143:4">143:4</a> My strength leaves me;
> I am absolutely shocked.
> <a name="19:143:5">143:5</a> I recall the old days;
> I meditate on all you have done;
> I reflect on your accomplishments.
> <a name="19:143:6">143:6</a> I spread my hands out to you in prayer;
> my soul thirsts for you in a parched land.
> <a name="19:143:7">143:7</a> Answer me quickly, Lord!
> My strength is fading.
> Do not reject me,
> or I will join those descending into the grave.
> <a name="19:143:8">143:8</a> May I hear about your loyal love in the morning,
> for I trust in you.
> Show me the way I should go,
> because I long for you.
> <a name="19:143:9">143:9</a> Rescue me from my enemies, O Lord!
> I run to you for protection.
> <a name="19:143:10">143:10</a> Teach me to do what pleases you,
> for you are my God.
> May your kind presence
> lead me into a level land.
> <a name="19:143:11">143:11</a> O Lord, for the sake of your reputation, revive me!
> Because of your justice, rescue me from trouble!
> <a name="19:143:12">143:12</a> As a demonstration of your loyal love, destroy my enemies!
> Annihilate all who threaten my life,
> for I am your servant.

### Psalm 144

By David.

> <a name="19:144:1">144:1</a> The Lord, my protector, deserves praise—
> the one who trains my hands for battle,
> and my fingers for war,
> <a name="19:144:2">144:2</a> who loves me and is my stronghold,
> my refuge and my deliverer,
> my shield and the one in whom I take shelter,
> who makes nations submit to me.
> <a name="19:144:3">144:3</a> O Lord, “Of what importance is the human race, that you should notice them?
> Of what importance is mankind, that you should be concerned about them?
> <a name="19:144:4">144:4</a> People are like a vapor,
> their days like a shadow that disappears.
> <a name="19:144:5">144:5</a> O Lord, make the sky sink and come down!
> Touch the mountains and make them smolder!
> <a name="19:144:6">144:6</a> Hurl lightning bolts and scatter them!
> Shoot your arrows and rout them!
> <a name="19:144:7">144:7</a> Reach down from above!
> Grab me and rescue me from the surging water,
> from the power of foreigners,
> <a name="19:144:8">144:8</a> who speak lies,
> and make false promises.
> <a name="19:144:9">144:9</a> O God, I will sing a new song to you!
> Accompanied by a ten-stringed instrument, I will sing praises to you,
> <a name="19:144:10">144:10</a> the one who delivers kings,
> and rescued David his servant from a deadly sword.
> <a name="19:144:11">144:11</a> Grab me and rescue me from the power of foreigners,
> who speak lies,
> and make false promises.
> <a name="19:144:12">144:12</a> Then our sons will be like plants,
> that quickly grow to full size.
> Our daughters will be like corner pillars,
> carved like those in a palace.
> <a name="19:144:13">144:13</a> Our storehouses will be full,
> providing all kinds of food.
> Our sheep will multiply by the thousands
> and fill our pastures.
> <a name="19:144:14">144:14</a> Our cattle will be weighted down with produce.
> No one will break through our walls,
> no one will be taken captive,
> and there will be no terrified cries in our city squares.
> <a name="19:144:15">144:15</a> How happy are the people who experience these things!
> How happy are the people whose God is the Lord!

### Psalm 145

A psalm of praise, by David.

> <a name="19:145:1">145:1</a> I will extol you, my God, O king!
> I will praise your name continually!
> <a name="19:145:2">145:2</a> Every day I will praise you!
> I will praise your name continually!
> <a name="19:145:3">145:3</a> The Lord is great and certainly worthy of praise!
> No one can fathom his greatness!
> <a name="19:145:4">145:4</a> One generation will praise your deeds to another,
> and tell about your mighty acts!
> <a name="19:145:5">145:5</a> I will focus on your honor and majestic splendor,
> and your amazing deeds!
> <a name="19:145:6">145:6</a> They will proclaim the power of your awesome acts!
> I will declare your great deeds!
> <a name="19:145:7">145:7</a> They will talk about the fame of your great kindness,
> and sing about your justice.
> <a name="19:145:8">145:8</a> The Lord is merciful and compassionate;
> he is patient and demonstrates great loyal love.
> <a name="19:145:9">145:9</a> The Lord is good to all,
> and has compassion on all he has made.
> <a name="19:145:10">145:10</a> All he has made will give thanks to the Lord.
> Your loyal followers will praise you.
> <a name="19:145:11">145:11</a> They will proclaim the splendor of your kingdom;
> they will tell about your power,
> <a name="19:145:12">145:12</a> so that mankind might acknowledge your mighty acts,
> and the majestic splendor of your kingdom.
> <a name="19:145:13">145:13</a> Your kingdom is an eternal kingdom,
> and your dominion endures through all generations.
> <a name="19:145:14">145:14</a> The Lord supports all who fall,
> and lifts up all who are bent over.
> <a name="19:145:15">145:15</a> Everything looks to you in anticipation,
> and you provide them with food on a regular basis.
> <a name="19:145:16">145:16</a> You open your hand,
> and fill every living thing with the food they desire.
> <a name="19:145:17">145:17</a> The Lord is just in all his actions,
> and exhibits love in all he does.
> <a name="19:145:18">145:18</a> The Lord is near all who cry out to him,
> all who cry out to him sincerely.
> <a name="19:145:19">145:19</a> He satisfies the desire of his loyal followers;
> he hears their cry for help and delivers them.
> <a name="19:145:20">145:20</a> The Lord protects those who love him,
> but he destroys all the wicked.
> <a name="19:145:21">145:21</a> My mouth will praise the Lord.
> Let all who live praise his holy name forever!

### Psalm 146

> <a name="19:146:1">146:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Praise the Lord, O my soul!
> <a name="19:146:2">146:2</a> I will praise the Lord as long as I live!
> I will sing praises to my God as long as I exist!
> <a name="19:146:3">146:3</a> Do not trust in princes,
> or in human beings, who cannot deliver!
> <a name="19:146:4">146:4</a> Their life’s breath departs, they return to the ground;
> on that day their plans die.
> <a name="19:146:5">146:5</a> How happy is the one whose helper is the God of Jacob,
> whose hope is in the Lord his God,
> <a name="19:146:6">146:6</a> the one who made heaven and earth,
> the sea, and all that is in them,
> who remains forever faithful,
> <a name="19:146:7">146:7</a> vindicates the oppressed,
> and gives food to the hungry.
> The Lord releases the imprisoned.
> <a name="19:146:8">146:8</a> The Lord gives sight to the blind.
> The Lord lifts up all who are bent over.
> The Lord loves the godly.
> <a name="19:146:9">146:9</a> The Lord protects those residing outside their native land;
> he lifts up the fatherless and the widow,
> but he opposes the wicked.
> <a name="19:146:10">146:10</a> The Lord rules forever,
> your God, O Zion, throughout the generations to come!
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 147

> <a name="19:147:1">147:1</a> Praise the Lord,
> for it is good to sing praises to our God!
> Yes, praise is pleasant and appropriate!
> <a name="19:147:2">147:2</a> The Lord rebuilds Jerusalem,
> and gathers the exiles of Israel.
> <a name="19:147:3">147:3</a> He heals the brokenhearted,
> and bandages their wounds.
> <a name="19:147:4">147:4</a> He counts the number of the stars;
> he names all of them.
> <a name="19:147:5">147:5</a> Our sovereign Master is great and has awesome power;
> there is no limit to his wisdom.
> <a name="19:147:6">147:6</a> The Lord lifts up the oppressed,
> but knocks the wicked to the ground.
> <a name="19:147:7">147:7</a> Offer to the Lord a song of thanks!
> Sing praises to our God to the accompaniment of a harp!
> <a name="19:147:8">147:8</a> He covers the sky with clouds,
> provides the earth with rain,
> and causes grass to grow on the hillsides.
> <a name="19:147:9">147:9</a> He gives food to the animals,
> and to the young ravens when they chirp.
> <a name="19:147:10">147:10</a> He is not enamored with the strength of a horse,
> nor is he impressed by the warrior’s strong legs.
> <a name="19:147:11">147:11</a> The Lord takes delight in his faithful followers,
> and in those who wait for his loyal love.
> <a name="19:147:12">147:12</a> Extol the Lord, O Jerusalem!
> Praise your God, O Zion!
> <a name="19:147:13">147:13</a> For he makes the bars of your gates strong.
> He blesses your children within you.
> <a name="19:147:14">147:14</a> He brings peace to your territory.
> He abundantly provides for you the best grain.
> <a name="19:147:15">147:15</a> He sends his command through the earth;
> swiftly his order reaches its destination.
> <a name="19:147:16">147:16</a> He sends the snow that is white like wool;
> he spreads the frost that is white like ashes.
> <a name="19:147:17">147:17</a> He throws his hailstones like crumbs.
> Who can withstand the cold wind he sends?
> <a name="19:147:18">147:18</a> He then orders it all to melt;
> he breathes on it, and the water flows.
> <a name="19:147:19">147:19</a> He proclaims his word to Jacob,
> his statutes and regulations to Israel.
> <a name="19:147:20">147:20</a> He has not done so with any other nation;
> they are not aware of his regulations.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 148

> <a name="19:148:1">148:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Praise the Lord from the sky!
> Praise him in the heavens!
> <a name="19:148:2">148:2</a> Praise him, all his angels!
> Praise him, all his heavenly assembly!
> <a name="19:148:3">148:3</a> Praise him, O sun and moon!
> Praise him, all you shiny stars!
> <a name="19:148:4">148:4</a> Praise him, O highest heaven,
> and you waters above the sky!
> <a name="19:148:5">148:5</a> Let them praise the name of the Lord,
> for he gave the command and they came into existence.
> <a name="19:148:6">148:6</a> He established them so they would endure;
> he issued a decree that will not be revoked.
> <a name="19:148:7">148:7</a> Praise the Lord from the earth,
> you sea creatures and all you ocean depths,
> <a name="19:148:8">148:8</a> O fire and hail, snow and clouds,
> O stormy wind that carries out his orders,
> <a name="19:148:9">148:9</a> you mountains and all you hills,
> you fruit trees and all you cedars,
> <a name="19:148:10">148:10</a> you animals and all you cattle,
> you creeping things and birds,
> <a name="19:148:11">148:11</a> you kings of the earth and all you nations,
> you princes and all you leaders on the earth,
> <a name="19:148:12">148:12</a> you young men and young women,
> you elderly, along with you children!
> <a name="19:148:13">148:13</a> Let them praise the name of the Lord,
> for his name alone is exalted;
> his majesty extends over the earth and sky.
> <a name="19:148:14">148:14</a> He has made his people victorious,
> and given all his loyal followers reason to praise—
> the Israelites, the people who are close to him.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 149

> <a name="19:149:1">149:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Sing to the Lord a new song!
> Praise him in the assembly of the godly!
> <a name="19:149:2">149:2</a> Let Israel rejoice in their Creator!
> Let the people of Zion delight in their king!
> <a name="19:149:3">149:3</a> Let them praise his name with dancing!
> Let them sing praises to him to the accompaniment of the tambourine and harp!
> <a name="19:149:4">149:4</a> For the Lord takes delight in his people;
> he exalts the oppressed by delivering them.
> <a name="19:149:5">149:5</a> Let the godly rejoice because of their vindication!
> Let them shout for joy upon their beds!
> <a name="19:149:6">149:6</a> May they praise God
> while they hold a two-edged sword in their hand,
> <a name="19:149:7">149:7</a> in order to take revenge on the nations,
> and punish foreigners.
> <a name="19:149:8">149:8</a> They bind their kings in chains,
> and their nobles in iron shackles,
> <a name="19:149:9">149:9</a> and execute the judgment to which their enemies have been sentenced.
> All his loyal followers will be vindicated.
> Praise the Lord!

### Psalm 150

> <a name="19:150:1">150:1</a> Praise the Lord!
> Praise God in his sanctuary!
> Praise him in the sky, which testifies to his strength!
> <a name="19:150:2">150:2</a> Praise him for his mighty acts!
> Praise him for his surpassing greatness!
> <a name="19:150:3">150:3</a> Praise him with the blast of the horn!
> Praise him with the lyre and the harp!
> <a name="19:150:4">150:4</a> Praise him with the tambourine and with dancing!
> Praise him with stringed instruments and the flute!
> <a name="19:150:5">150:5</a> Praise him with loud cymbals!
> Praise him with clanging cymbals!
> <a name="19:150:6">150:6</a> Let everything that has breath praise the Lord!
> Praise the Lord!
